Roosevelt Issues Decree for Concrete Reorganization of the Recovery Administration

Appointing Two Committees to Oversee the Matter

Lee Shipherd Succeeds Johnson as Leader

(Washington) President Roosevelt issued two decrees at the White House today. These are the first concrete actions taken by the president to reorganize the Recovery Administration. In the first decree, the president appointed a six-member committee, with Lee Shipherd, an advisor to the Recovery Administration, as chairman. After the reorganization, the committee will draft national recovery policies. The second decree appointed a five-member committee to take over the vacancy left by General Johnson. Johnson's resignation will take effect on October 15th. The two committees appointed by the president will share the control formerly exercised by Johnson since the establishment of the National Recovery Administration. The committee led by Lee Shipherd will be the highest authority for deciding recovery policies. The second committee will implement the policies set by the first committee. (27th National Electric)

(New York) The fact that Lee Shipherd will serve as the chairman of the design committee for the Recovery Administration was discussed by Nicer, who is familiar with the affairs of the administration, in an article in the New York Commercial Bulletin today. He stated that the hope that the administration's policies would be overseen by those familiar with the real situation of industry has been completely extinguished. Because all the members of the committee are leftist government officials, the beneficiaries will be laborers, farmers, and consumers. They do not understand industry and will inevitably prioritize their interests. The appointed members have clearly indicated that the government cannot move to the right. Since the executive committee can only implement the policies set by the design committee, the representatives of the industry will have no choice but to be helpless. (27th National Electric)

(Washington) Political and economic experts stated today that President Roosevelt has apparently rejected General Johnson's proposal that the government gradually withdraw its control over private industry. Lee Shipherd's appointment as chairman of the design committee for the Recovery Administration clearly indicates that Roosevelt still intends to control industry through the Recovery Act. Therefore, the proposals of government leaders such as Lee Shipherd and Labor Secretary Perkins have been supported by the president. The design committee has now been authorized by the president to formulate all the policies of the Recovery Administration. It is noteworthy that all the members of the design committee are enthusiastic supporters of the New Deal. (27th National Electric)

(Washington) President Roosevelt recently announced the general outline of the plan to reorganize the Economic Recovery Bureau. According to this plan, the Recovery Bureau will lose most of its autonomy and will be subject to closer supervision by cabinet members and the heads of special agencies dealing with industrial, labor, and social issues. President Roosevelt himself retains the power to approve all important decisions. The president has appointed three committees in accordance with this plan. (1) The Industrial Emergency Committee is responsible for formulating general policies and legislative matters regarding economic recovery. The committee has six members, with Lee Shipherd, an advisor to the Economic Recovery Bureau, as chairman. The other members are Interior Secretary Ickes, Labor Secretary Perkins, Agricultural Adjustment Administration Director Davis, Federal Relief Bureau Director Hopkins, and the sixth member is the chairman of the five-member committee below, who will be elected by the committee itself. (2) The five-member committee is responsible for the administrative affairs of the Recovery Act, also known as the National Industrial Recovery Board. It will work under the guidance of President Roosevelt. The members are not well-known, but they have all actively assisted in the organization of the Economic Recovery Bureau. Two of the members are industrialists, Williams and Whiteside. The other two are labor representatives, Hillman, the president of the New York Clothing Workers' Union, and lawyer Marshall. The fifth member is Yale University law professor Hamilton. Roosevelt also appointed Smith, the legal advisor to the Economic Recovery Bureau, and Henderson, the economic advisor, as advisors to the committee for consultation. The committee members will elect the chairman from among themselves. It is likely to be Colonel Lynch, a friend of General Johnson. (3) The third committee is responsible for judicial issues and is responsible for supervising the implementation of the Recovery Bureau's procedures and resolutions. The members have not yet been designated. Since Lee Shipherd is currently serving as the secretary of the Executive Council of the President and the chairman of the National Emergency Committee, and he is now also appointed as the chairman of the Industrial Emergency Committee, he has become the main executor of President Roosevelt's will on various industrial and social issues. (29th Havas Electric)

(Washington) Three thousand women held a meeting in New York today to discuss current issues. President Roosevelt addressed them via radio, saying that the people's attention to national affairs is one of the most optimistic things in the recovery movement. The President also said that the fact that the people can think and act for themselves, and that rumor-mongers cannot cause trouble, is greatly beneficial to the country and is something we should be most grateful for. The President concluded by saying that our people have already taken a firm foothold and are moving forward. The current affairs discussion meeting held by the three thousand women in New York was sponsored by the newspaper and forum. (27th National Electric)

US Federal Reserve Advisory Council

Advocates for Restoration of the Gold Standard

Submits Six Proposals

Chicago The Federal Reserve Advisory Council sent a letter to Thomas, Acting Director of the Federal Reserve Board, today, requesting the early restoration of the gold standard, stating that the restoration of the gold standard is a prerequisite for restoring lasting prosperity. The Advisory Council's action today is the same as its recommendation last November. The Advisory Council today advocated the following: (1) Fluctuations in currency hinder commercial development. (2) Formulating a balanced budget is necessary for restoring public trust. (3) Government money should stop competing with private capital. (4) Excessive government debt endangers public credit. (5) The current currency and pledges are sufficient to circulate for commercial expansion, so the demands of the inflationists are completely without sufficient reason. (6) The situation is stable and commerce can recover its original state. (27th National Electric)

Hoover's New Book Published

Attacks Roosevelt's New Deal

(New York) Former President Hoover's book, "The Challenge to Liberty," was published here today. Hoover has recently published articles in the Saturday Evening Post, and the book is a supplement to those articles. It severely attacks President Roosevelt's "New Deal," saying that the principles of the "New Deal" have no boundaries, and claiming that Roosevelt is leading the United States down the path to a dictatorship, so that the traditional freedom of the American people has been almost completely deprived. Therefore, he urged the American people to carefully consider the consequences of Congress's complete submission to the President, and asked the people not to repeat the mistakes of the past. Literary critics have reacted coldly to the book, believing that it is too profound for the average person to understand. (27th National Electric)

The Middle East Railway Deal

Japan and Russia Agree on Selling Price

The News is Acknowledged by Moscow

Whether a Deal is Reached Depends on Detailed Negotiations

(Moscow) Well-informed sources here acknowledged today that the purchase price of the Chinese Eastern Railway has been agreed upon. However, Moscow views these successful negotiations as a preliminary step for the Soviet Union and the (Manchurian) authorities to reopen formal discussions on the issue. It is said that the recent resumption of negotiations in Tokyo was proposed by the Japanese side, which agreed to pay a higher price than before. The final success of these negotiations, from the Soviet perspective, depends on the outcome of discussions on several details, such as how the purchase price will be paid and how Soviet personnel will be handled in the future. (Reuters, 27th)

France Raises Reservations

The Hague News: Regarding the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway by the Soviet Union, rumors say that Japan and the Soviet Union have reached a basic agreement. Upon receiving this news, financial circles are rumored to say that the French government immediately notified Moscow and Tokyo that it reserves its rights regarding the interests of the French side in the Chinese Eastern Railway. (Havas, 28th)

British Newspaper Commentary (London) Regarding the possibility of Japan and Russia reaching an agreement on the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, The Times, not having received official information, is unwilling to comment. However, it is quite pleased that Japan and Russia have room for compromise, stating: (Although the Soviet Union and Japan have not fully agreed on all points of contention regarding the Chinese Eastern Railway, the main points have been understood, and it seems unlikely that they will break down due to disputes over details. However, to say that Japan and Russia can now be completely aligned would be wishful thinking. The mutual suspicion between the two countries still exists. The Soviet Union has long suspected Japan of harboring territorial ambitions, and Japan and Russia compete with each other in Mongolia, their interests also conflicting. Conversely, Soviet communist propaganda in China, Korea, and even within Japan is enough to worry Japan. All of these things cannot be easily eliminated. What we are fortunate about is that the most intense dispute between the two countries, which could at any time lead to serious incidents in Manchuria, can now be resolved, and the tension in Japanese-Russian relations can be temporarily eased.)

Japanese Business Activities (Tokyo) Once the transfer negotiations for the Chinese Eastern Railway are concluded, part of the payment, approximately 100 million yuan worth of goods, must be transported to Russia. Therefore, many people have been visiting the Soviet Union Trade Agency every day to inquire about the goods needed. Similarly, many have been visiting the Trade Bureau to inquire about methods of selling to the Soviet Union. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has begun to study representative goods and has been in contact with the Ministry of Commerce and Industry, intending to establish a new path for Japanese-Russian trade, which has been on the verge of collapse. The goods to be delivered must be selected from the necessities of the Second Five-Year Plan and those that could not be produced during the First and Second Five-Year Plans. At the same time, issues such as credit arrangements, which have been problematic when the Soviet Union purchases Japanese goods, will be fully and concretely addressed. The export industry to Russia will take this opportunity to establish an organization and enjoy the financial convenience of large investment banking groups. Because individual negotiations and discussions are unlikely to be satisfactory, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs plans to establish a Japanese-Russian trade association to ensure fair and appropriate transactions, eliminating partial organizational structures. (Dentsu, 28th)

Shen Bao Third Edition

League of Nations Decides Not to Send Additional Personnel to China

Rajchman Appointed Director of the League of Nations Health Section

Guo Taiqi Describes Achievements of Technical Cooperation

(Geneva) Rajchman, who previously served as a technical advisor to the Chinese government, was appointed today as the director of the League of Nations Health Section for a term of seven years. The Committee on Technical Cooperation with China has decided not to send additional personnel to China, but will send heads of various departments to China when needed. (Reuters, 28th)

(Geneva) The Committee on Technical Cooperation between the League of Nations and China met today. After a presentation by Chinese representative Guo Taiqi, it listened to the opinions of various technical agencies of the League of Nations regarding the report submitted by Dr. Rajchman, the League of Nations Liaison Officer for Technical Cooperation with China. Dr. Rajchman submitted this report to the various technical agencies of the League of Nations in accordance with the resolution of the Executive Yuan's Committee on Technical Cooperation between the League of Nations and China on March 17 of this year. The technical agencies will then submit written opinions to the committee and take or prepare to take various measures within their scope of authority to promote technical cooperation between the League of Nations and China. The committee declared that the various technical agencies of the League of Nations are prepared to continue actively assisting this endeavor, as it is given special importance by the Executive Yuan. In addition, the League of Nations Intellectual Cooperation Organization will provide assistance to the job placement services for Chinese intellectuals and technicians. The Chinese government has decided to establish such job placement offices in Nanjing and the West to make it easier for Chinese students studying in Europe and America to obtain vocational training to meet the current needs of China's economic construction. The committee paid particular attention to this fact. As for the League of Nations Health Organization and its experts, they have assisted the Chinese government in implementing a three-year plan established in 1930 to develop the Central Hygiene Facilities Experimental Office and have recently assisted in various health and veterinary projects in the inland provinces. The Transportation and Transit Organization is inclined towards highways and water conservancy, cooperating with the Chinese National Economic Council. A team of experts appointed by the Transportation and Transit Organization will soon go to the interior of China at the request of the Chinese government to conduct a thorough investigation of several issues related to water conservancy and highways. Dr. Rajchman's report stated that, with the exception of a few specialized departments, the number of Chinese citizens suitable for participating in the country's economic construction is increasing daily. The committee, upon hearing this, believes that if the Chinese government and its experts can make the most of other countries' administrative and institutional experience, this progress can be accelerated. Finally, the task assigned to Dr. Rajchman, the League of Nations Liaison Officer for Technical Cooperation with China, expired on August 1 of this year. He returned to his original position as Director of the Health Section of the League of Nations Secretariat. The committee specifically approved this and thanked Dr. Rajchman for his excellent performance. The committee believes that it is not yet necessary to appoint a technical liaison officer to succeed Rajchman at this time, but requests the League of Nations Secretariat to take necessary measures to ensure the continued development of various technical cooperation projects. (Havas, 28th)

Britain, France, and Italy Issue Joint Declaration on Austrian Affairs

Austrian Independence as a Common Standard of Policy for the Three Countries

The Little Entente Countries Will Study This Declaration at Length

(Geneva) Britain, France, and Italy have been consulting for a long time on the issue of jointly guaranteeing Austrian independence. Tonight, the three countries jointly issued a declaration stating (The representatives of France, Britain, and Italy have re-examined the situation in Austria).

Afterwards, they mutually agreed to recognize, in the name of their respective governments, the declaration issued on February 17, 1934, by the three countries to maintain Austrian independence and territorial integrity, which remains fully effective and continues to be the common standard of policy for the three countries). (Havas, 27th)

(Geneva) Britain, France, and Italy signed a joint declaration today, reaffirming the three countries' determination to maintain the independence and territorial integrity of Austria, thus giving more force to the three countries' statement of February 17th of this year. The declaration was signed by British Minister Lord Earl, French Foreign Minister Barthou, and Italian Count Aloisi. Britain and France had already agreed on the content of the declaration yesterday, but it was delayed until today pending Italian approval. Although the declaration does not specify which country it is aimed at, it is internally aimed at Germany. However, there is much speculation as to what extent it will be implemented. (National, 27th)

(Geneva) The British government's willingness to sign the tripartite declaration was due to the special request of French Foreign Minister Barthou. Barthou expressed great satisfaction with Britain's decision, as this move could dispel all rumors of discord between Britain, France, and Italy on the Austrian issue. The declaration has now been sent to the Little Entente countries, and those who wish to join may also sign it. It is generally believed that the three countries' compromise on Austria is timely, as the current session of the League of Nations Assembly will end tomorrow. (Reuters, 27th)

(Geneva) Czech Foreign Minister Benes declared that the joint declaration issued by Britain, France, and Italy to guarantee Austrian independence is based on the statement of February 17 of this year. He also said that the Little Entente countries will study this declaration at length and consider how to participate in this declaration in the future. (Havas, 27th)

Vienna: The semi-official Federal Postal Gazette here published an important article, which is generally believed to be written by Prime Minister Schuschnigg. The article reviews the truth of the negotiations on the Austrian independence issue in Geneva, stating that this matter was not initiated by Austria and that Austria has always been passive in this matter. The article states that Austria's movement for independent autonomy to determine its future has not been affected and that Austria will never forget that another Germanic nation and its foreign policy must be in harmony with the beliefs held by the Austrian people. This is the first time that doubts have been expressed here about Italy's interests in Austrian diplomacy. (National, 27th)

Vienna: People in Vienna, except for the Pan-Germanists, are satisfied with the joint declaration on Austrian independence issued by Britain, France, and Italy in Geneva. The Wiener Zeitung stated that the declaration in Geneva is a clear and forceful warning to anyone who wants to violate Austria. The Neue Wiener Tagblatt stated that foreign politicians have given endless benefits to European peace with clear words and strong postures, for which we should be grateful. (Havas, 28th)

Poland Does Not Participate in the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact

Reply Sent to the French Government

However, the Door to Negotiations Is Not Closed

(Geneva) Poland's reply to the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact issue has now been sent to the French government. Its content is merely a written summary of the talks between Barthou and Beck, which cannot be made public at present. The content of the reply roughly states that Poland cannot approve of the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact in its current form. The document also lists the treaties Poland has signed with France, Germany, and the Soviet Union, stating that Poland's foreign policy seeks to establish friendly relations with various European countries. As for whether the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact can provide Poland with greater security, the Polish government has doubts about this. However, negotiations can still be conducted in the future. This reply does not close the door to negotiations. (Havas, 27th)

Ecuador Joins the League of Nations

Membership Now at Sixty Countries

(Geneva) Ecuador officially joined the League of Nations today, bringing the League's membership to sixty countries, the highest number since the League's establishment. The 82nd session of the League of Nations Executive Council was declared closed. (National, 27th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council met this morning. League of Nations Secretary General Avenol announced that the United States and Ecuador have decided to join the League of Nations. Ecuador is one of the founding member states listed in the Covenant of the League of Nations attached to the Treaty of Versailles, so Ecuador's accession to the League of Nations does not require any further procedures. Representatives from Mexico, Chile, and Portugal, as well as the acting chairman of the Executive Council, Czech Ambassador to France Ossusky, spoke, expressing their satisfaction with Ecuador's accession. At this point, the Ecuadorian representative entered the meeting hall and declared that his country was deeply pleased to join the League of Nations and contribute to the cause of peace. (Havas, 27th)

League of Nations Executive Council Discusses Saar Issue

And Begins Negotiations with Germany

French Foreign Minister Issues Declaration

Does Not Give Up Its Rights

(Geneva) French Foreign Minister Barthou announced today at a meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council that France would not hesitate to send a large army into the Saar region to maintain order. Barthou usually spoke extemporaneously, but this time he read from a prepared text, so his remarks were particularly emphasized. Barthou said that France had not given up any of its rights in the Saar, but would naturally abide by the results of the plebiscite to be held next year in the Saar region. If the Saar Governing Commission cannot guarantee the fairness of the plebiscite due to insufficient police force, the French government is prepared to provide it. (Reuters, 27th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Executive Council convened a meeting today to discuss the Saar issue. First, Aloisi, Chairman of the Committee of Three, submitted a report on the preparations for the Saar region's vote of self-determination to the General Assembly. Aloisi stated that an increase in security forces during the open vote next year is necessary to maintain public order at that time. Therefore, the Committee of Three needs to request additional funding from both Germany and France. French Foreign Minister Barthou then rose and delivered a very long declaration, stating that the Committee's work is divided into two major parts: one is the preparation for the open vote, and the other is the various issues after the vote. Barthou also stated that it is regrettable that a suitable solution has not yet been found regarding the issue of maintaining public order in the Saar region and that the situation in the Saar is very serious, as discovered by the League of Nations Governing Commission. Barthou continued, stating that France is deeply concerned about this matter because France may inevitably have to assume special responsibilities as future events unfold. Therefore, if this danger is to be avoided, the Saar Governing Commission must have sufficient financial resources to expand its security forces. The people in the Saar region must first understand, before the vote, what the effects will be if they support maintaining the status quo. Barthou insisted that it is the responsibility of the League of Nations Council to make the people in the Saar region understand this point, and that this work is urgent because the voters in the Saar region must understand the meaning of each solution as soon as possible. Therefore, Barthou advocated that this issue must be addressed at an extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations convened in China in November. (National, 27th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations and Germany began negotiations today on the Saar problem, hoping to reach a practical compromise on the issue in November of this year. At the same time, the work of the League of Nations Executive Council in reviewing the report of the Saar Governing Commission concluded this afternoon, and it was decided to convene another special meeting of the Executive Council on November 15 to deal with this matter. Among the various minor issues discussed with Germany so far, the most difficult is the recruitment of police to maintain order during the plebiscite. Germany strongly argued that there is no need to recruit police from outside the region, and if the Executive Council insists on recruiting them, Germany cannot be held responsible for the consequences. However, the League of Nations also did not show weakness on this point, firmly intending to implement the request of Knox, Chairman of the Saar Governing Commission. Knox previously applied to the League of Nations Executive Council on the 14th of this month to recruit 2,000 police officers from foreign countries to strengthen the Saar's police force, as the Saar currently has only 1,000 police officers, which is not enough to dispatch during the plebiscite. (Reuters, 27th)

League of Nations Assembly Concludes

Representatives Partially Return Home

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly has begun to conclude all the items on the agenda tonight, in order to announce its closure. Some of the representatives of various countries have already returned home, and the rest will depart soon. Soviet Foreign Minister Litvinov and Polish Foreign Minister Beck have both left here tonight, while French Foreign Minister Barthou is scheduled to return home tomorrow night. (Havas, 27th)

(Geneva) The League of Nations Assembly passed various reports discussed and approved by the sub-committees today and then announced its closure.

Japanese Cabinet Formally Decides to Convene Extraordinary Diet Session

Date of Convocation Not Determined

Scope of Proposals Limited to Disaster Relief

The Anti-Counterfeiting Reform Bill May Not Be on the Agenda

Hirota Will Explain Diplomatic Policy

(Tokyo) Today's regular cabinet meeting was held at the Prime Minister's residence at 10:20 AM. After all cabinet members, including Prime Minister Okada, were present, Minister of Home Affairs Goto first reported in detail on the state of the disaster in the Kansai region, which took about 55 minutes. He then argued that because the disaster was so severe, an extraordinary Diet session must be convened to establish relief measures. (3) Regarding the provision of low-interest funds, it must be stated that there is an urgent and appropriate purpose. (Dentsu, 28th)

He plans to explain in detail the progress of Japan's important diplomatic issues since the ordinary Diet session this spring and clarify the Japanese government's diplomatic policy both domestically and abroad. The main points of the Foreign Minister's speech are as follows:

In addition to explaining the above situation, he will especially focus on the naval conference and the determination to establish peace among Japan, Britain, and the United States. (Nichi-Ren, 28th)

(Tokyo) The government will only discuss emergency relief measures for typhoon and drought-stricken areas and poor sericulture areas at the extraordinary Diet session. Whether it is as urgent as the former is also debatable, so its decision will inevitably cause considerable waves, and deliberation will also take a considerable amount of time. Also, rice countermeasures should be carefully deliberated by the ordinary Diet in nature, so it is also unwilling to put it on the agenda of the extraordinary Diet session. (Dentsu, 28th)

(Tokyo) Regarding the date of convening the extraordinary meeting, Minister of Finance Fujii stated at the cabinet meeting on the 28th that it would be difficult to convene it in mid-October due to administrative reasons, but the opinion of holding the meeting earlier was prevalent. Hopeman's Re-trial: Lindbergh Attends Court

Hong Kong Hit by Gale and Torrential Rain

Typhoon Shifts, Strikes Annam Coast

(Hong Kong) Hong Kong was hit by gale-force winds and torrential rain late on the 27th. The seas were turbulent. The intensity began to subside slightly on the morning of the 28th. The Observatory removed Typhoon Signal No. 1 today. A report issued at 10:00 AM stated that the typhoon, located between 109 degrees East longitude and 17 degrees North latitude, had shifted and was now striking the coast of Annam, with no impact on Hainan Island. (Central News Agency dispatch, 28th)

Reason for the Return of Hot Weather

(Nanjing) According to the Nanjing Meteorological Institute, since the beginning of autumn, the weather has been gradually cooling. However, on the 28th, it suddenly became hot again, humid, and foggy. The highest temperature was 90.05 degrees Fahrenheit. This is due to a low-pressure system situated over the lower reaches of the Yellow River, while a high-pressure system from the Pacific Ocean has extended into southeastern China. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River are within the range of both pressure systems, resulting in southerly and southeasterly winds, few clouds, and strong sunshine, creating muggy conditions. A hurricane was recently discovered in the Pacific Ocean, south of the Philippines. Whether it will affect China's coastal areas depends on whether its direction changes. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Examination Expenses for Trial Officials: Funds to be Drawn as Planned

(Nanjing) The examination expenses for trial officials, compiled by the Ministry of Justice in the provisional budget for the 23rd year, are planned to be drawn from the first reserve fund under the heading of judicial expenses in the approved national expenditure, amounting to four thousand yuan. The Directorate General of Budgets, Accounting and Statistics has approved the filing. The National Government, on the 27th, ordered the Executive Yuan and the Control Yuan to instruct the Ministries of Finance, Justice, and Audit to take note. (Central News Agency dispatch, 28th)

Mei Siping Concurrently Appointed Jiangning Security Commander

(Nanjing) The Jiangsu Provincial Government has appointed Mei Siping, the Magistrate of Jiangning County, to concurrently serve as the Commander of Security for Jiangning. He took office on the 28th. Nanjing Social Affairs Bureau Offers Rural Civilian Loans

(Nanjing) The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau is offering rural civilian loans, in consultation with Jin Cheng Bank. (Special dispatch, 28th)

No Government Control Over Foreign Trade

(Nanjing) Liang Shangdong, the Director of the Commercial Affairs Department of the Ministry of Industry, stated that reports claiming the government is planning to promote various industries and commerce and facilitate their overseas sales are largely misunderstandings. According to him, China does not implement control over foreign trade. Overseas Chinese, concerned about the poor performance of domestic industry and commerce, have sent representatives back to China for investigation. The government cannot ignore this and is only planning ways to promote the sale of domestic goods. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Ministry of Interior Investigates Civil Servants Smoking Opium

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Interior has informed various provinces and municipalities to investigate civil servants who smoke opium and submit reports for disciplinary action. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Ministry of Communications Transfers Yu Senwen to England

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Communications has ordered the transfer of Yu Senwen, Director of the Labor Affairs Committee, to serve as a specialist for the International Telegraph Bureau stationed in England. Chen Shaoxian, a member of the Legal Regulations Committee, has been appointed to fill the vacant position. Yu has departed for Shanghai to prepare for his journey, and Chen has also attended meetings to take up his duties. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Economic Committee's Expenses for Entertaining League of Nations Experts Approved

(Nanjing) The Economic Committee, in order to wholeheartedly entertain League of Nations experts who are coming to China to assist in promoting various undertakings, has had its entertainment expenses from last year, which were paid from monthly government allocations, approved to continue this year as the work is not yet completed. A budget has been prepared according to the old amount, estimating the entertainment expenses for the 23rd year to be 48,000 yuan. The Central Political Council has approved drawing this amount from the second reserve fund of the general budget. The National Government issued an order yesterday to inform the relevant departments. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Jingdezhen Porcelain Industry Representatives Petition Executive Yuan Again

(Nanjing) The Jingdezhen Porcelain Industry Association of Jiangxi Province, due to the excessively heavy taxation imposed by the Jiangxi Provincial Government, has repeatedly requested a reduction without success. They have again telegraphed representatives to personally petition the Executive Yuan, earnestly requesting a telegraphic order to stop the taxation. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Traffic Interrupted at Gubeikou, Beiping

(Beiping) Due to flooding this summer, the two main highways from Beiping to Gubeikou and to Jixian have been washed away, disrupting traffic for two months. After repairs, today's continuous rainfall has again damaged the two roads, disrupting traffic again. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Shandong People's Military Training Association Formulates One-Year Plan

(Jinan) The Shandong People's Military Training Association has formulated a one-year plan: 1. Stabilize the livelihoods of instructors in various schools; 2. Implement military-style management in schools, with committees dispatched to inspect; 3. Prepare for centralization; 4. Next year, centralize first-year high school students and above for three months of training. He Siyuan, the Director of the Education Department, has ordered all high schools to practice hiking and mountain climbing on October 10th. He himself will go to Mount Tai to lead. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Japanese Combined Fleet Arrives in Qingdao

(Qingdao) The Japanese 1st and 2nd Fleets, totaling seventy ships, led by Commander-in-Chief Suetsugu, entered the port in the rain at 1:00 PM on the 28th, mooring in the front and back harbors. The entire complement of officers and soldiers numbered 45,000. Commanders-in-Chief Suetsugu and Takahashi will go to Jinan tonight to meet Han. (Special dispatch, 28th)

(Qingdao) The Combined Fleet of over seventy ships, commanded by General Suetsugu, arrived here in full force from 8:00 AM to 1:00 PM today and will be stationed until October 3rd. Japanese expatriates made a special trip to the coast to express their welcome to the officers and men of the fleet. (Dentsu dispatch, 28th)

Shen Honglie to Accompany Han to Beiping

(Qingdao) Shen Honglie is scheduled to take the night express train to Jinan on the 2nd to accompany Han to Beiping to attend the Political Committee meeting. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Li Yizhi Flies from Lanzhou to Ningxia

(Kaifeng) The Yellow River Commission received a telegram from Li Yizhi stating that he flew from Lanzhou to Ningxia on the 26th to inspect along the river. The Red Swastika Society is promoting immigration to the Hetao region in Hua County, Changyuan, and Puyang. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Survey of Disaster-Stricken Counties in Hubei Province

(Hankou) A total of forty-nine counties in Hubei Province have been affected by the disaster, with thirty-seven counties being the most severely affected. The total value of food losses is over 88 million yuan, more than double the amount reported in June. The number of starving people on the verge of death has reached 3,520,000. The Disaster Relief Association is coordinating relief efforts and has scheduled a fundraising event for the 29th. (Special dispatch, 28th)

President of the Bank of Korea Arrives in Hankou

(Hankou) Kato Hujiro, the Japanese President of the Bank of Korea, along with staff members Maebashi and Kawai, arrived in Hankou by plane on the 28th. Their mission is unknown. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Hunan Drought Relief Association to be Established Soon

(Changsha) The Provincial Government has appointed gentry members Lei Mengqiang and others as members of the Drought Relief Association, scheduled to be established on the 1st. Each county's local defense units will be added. He Jian has ordered a reduction of eight jiao starting from the 24th year. He has appointed Yang Daonan and Cao Mingzhen as Deputy Commanders of the 1st and 2nd Security Districts. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Wuyongkang Industrial Company Opens

Wuzhou: The Yongkang Industrial Company, organized through investment from industrial circles in Guangxi and Shanghai, officially opened on the 27th. The ceremony was presided over by Chairman Guo Shun, Huang Zhongyue, Director of the Provincial Finance Department, and Zheng Yizhi, the General Manager. Numerous political and business figures attended. (Special dispatch, 27th)

Large Number of Criminals from Guanyun Escorted to Huai'an

(Qingjiangpu) Over a hundred criminals were recently transported from Guanyun by sailboats. Starting on the morning of the 28th, fifty-seven people, including Ma Shijie, were escorted into the city. For a time, the water gate and both sides of the ship bridge were heavily guarded, and traffic was cut off for about two hours. It is rumored that more criminals will arrive in the coming days. The local branch of the High Court has made adequate arrangements for the location. (Special dispatch, 28th)

Cai Bingyan Newly Appointed to Oversee Anhui Southern Defense Affairs

German Airline Company Prepares to Launch Berlin-Shanghai Air Route

(London) According to the Daily Express, the German Lufthansa airline company will launch an air route between Berlin and Shanghai next year. It is planned to pass through Greece, Persia, India, and southern China. It will be possible to fly from Europe to China in four days. The German side is currently negotiating transit issues with the relevant countries. As for the conditions along the way, they have already been surveyed by air. International Commercial Telegraph

丨Reuter's Special Commercial News Telegraph, September 28丨

Gold and Silver: London gold prices this morning (September 28) were 141 shillings and a halfpenny, down fourpence.

London silver market: spot prices rose 0.0625 to 22 pence and 4375, futures rose 0.125 to 22 pence and 5625. Market conditions were stable. India and speculators both bought and sold.

Bombay silver market: this morning, the silver market rose seven annas. Spot prices and October futures were both 61 rupees and ten annas, November futures were 61 rupees and twelve annas.

Exchange rates:

British-American: In the London foreign exchange market this morning, European countries slightly purchased British pounds due to the end of the month. The opening price was 4 dollars, 9 cents, and 6625, which was 25 lower than yesterday's closing price for British-American exchange rates. At 11 o'clock, it rose 5625 to 4 dollars, 9 cents, and 71875, but at noon, it fell 1875. At 1:00 PM, it returned 0625 to 4 dollars, 9 cents, and 70625. Trading was scarce at that time. The price did not change slightly at 2 o'clock. Also, one US dollar equals 4 lines of British gold and 0284. British-French: The opening price this morning was 74 francs 71, which was six pounds higher than yesterday's closing price. At 11 o'clock, it continued to rise 13 pounds to 74 francs 84. At noon, it fell six pounds. Until 2:00 PM, the price was still 74 francs 78.

American-British: In the New York foreign exchange market this morning, the opening price for American-British exchange rates rose 75 to 4 dollars, 9 cents, and 7625. But market conditions were quiet before noon. The price remained unchanged when the telegram was sent.

Cotton and Wheat:

New York cotton market: today (September 28), the cotton market opened with ups and downs of one pound each. At 10:30, it fell 45 pounds because spot merchants sold more and hedging also increased. At 10:40, the recent period recovered one pound.

New York wheat market: Due to poor news from Argentina and a lack of buyers, the wheat market opened down 50 to 75. But when the telegram was sent, the price was 25 to 3375 higher than the opening price.

Bombay cotton market: Today, the cotton market initially rose due to speculative buying and short covering, but then fell due to selling by European exporters and profit-taking by longs. Sentiment was still stable. The price for white cotton for the April-May period was 210 rupees 75, down two rupees.

Liverpool cotton market: today, the price for the January futures contract was 6.66, which was two pounds lower than yesterday's closing price.

Liverpool wheat market: Today, the price for the December futures contract at 1:00 PM rose 25 to 5 shillings, 5 pence, and 875.

Rubber:

London: Market conditions were stable today. The transaction price for October-December futures at noon was 7 pence and 375, the same as yesterday.

New York: London's telegrams were good, so the rubber market opened here, rising 8 to 13 pounds. Subsequently, due to profit-taking by longs, the price fell 1 to 6 pounds. When the telegram was sent, the December contract recovered 5 pounds.

Securities:

New York: Before the opening today, the factors favoring market conditions were: (1) The newly announced regulations on margin requirements for securities transactions are generally considered lenient, and some people say that, according to the methods stipulated in the new regulations, the amount of margin already paid is mostly excessive. (2) It is expected that President Roosevelt's speech on Sunday will be beneficial to market conditions, so sentiment is quite good. The unfavorable factor for market conditions is the instability of the government bond market. This morning, when securities opened, market conditions were narrow and uneven. Because the price rose yesterday, there was some speculative profit-taking this morning. Steel stocks were particularly under pressure. But everyone expects the rally to resume soon. The report for the first half of the year for the Anaconda Copper Mining Company estimates that the net profit for the first six months of this year was 2.986 million yuan, or 3.4 jiao per share. Great Disaster in Kansai Caused by Hurricane (Japanese News)

Wind Speed of Sixty Meters

Seven Prefectures Affected

At around 8:00 AM on September 21st, a hurricane struck the skies over Osaka City (a wind speed of over 30 meters is considered a hurricane). The speed was at least 40 meters and at most 60 meters. It was the most severe natural disaster since the Great Kanto Earthquake. When the hurricane struck, the sea tide also rose, and turbid currents ten feet high surged through the coastal areas. The local residents were shocked by the wind damage and also flooded. Fathers and sons were lost to each other, husbands and wives were separated, houses collapsed, and traffic was completely cut off. After 10:00, the gale gradually subsided, but Osaka, a place of brocade finery and towering smokestacks, truly a Japanese industrial center, instantly turned into the hell of wind and water.

According to a subsequent survey, the most severely affected areas were Osaka, followed by Kyoto, and then Hyogo, Kochi, Tottori, Ehime, and Okayama prefectures. When the hurricane occurred, it was during school hours, and most school buildings were not constructed very solidly, so they were easily damaged. This time, the number of collapsed school buildings was 146, with 528 deaths. Counting injured and missing teachers and students, there were a total of 2,245 people. The number of completely collapsed residences was 4,135 households. Counting partially collapsed houses, there were a total of 12,255 households. The total number of completely and partially collapsed non-residential buildings was 16,565. There were also 40 temples, shrines, government offices, etc. that were damaged. In total, the number of casualties was 4,650. One city tram was overturned, along with three trains. 1,627 large and small boats were lost.

In Kyoto Prefecture, 1,500 people were killed or injured. A total of 2,600 houses collapsed. Over 1,700 households were swept away or flooded.

In Hyogo Prefecture, 42,000 houses were flooded, and 1,677 households collapsed. There was damage to embankments at 146 locations. There were over 600 casualties, three landslides, 17 ships in distress, and 2,200 fishing boats. The other prefectures suffered relatively less damage and will not be described in detail.

Osaka is the industrial area of Japan, and (Konohana Ward), (Taisho Ward), and (Minato Ward) are the industrial zones of Osaka. All factories suffered major damage. However, the structure of the factories is very complex, especially military industries, so it is very difficult to calculate accurately. Moreover, there is a special secret military relationship among them. However, based on a general estimate, the losses in the factory areas of the aforementioned locations will be at least 300 million yen. The factories flooded in Konohana Ward, such as Liquid Air, Toyo Wood Preserving (drift loss), Osaka Iron, Sumitomo Copper Extrusion Steel Pipe, Sumitomo Steel, Sumitomo Electric Wire, Japan Dyestuff, Osaka Steel, Fuji Paper, Ajikawa Iron Works, Toa Iron Works, Osaka Leather Belt, Takeda Pharmaceutical, and Dai Nippon Artificial Fertilizer, etc., are mostly related to military industrial needs. The factories flooded in the Taisho Ward area include Toyo Spinning, Toyota Loom Casting, Fukan Steel Pipe, Osaka Steel Bar, Nakayama Steel, Imperial Artificial Fertilizer, and Hata Shipbuilding, etc. There were 800 flooded factories, and over 400 other small factories. About 80 factories belonging to Amagasaki were flooded, and production capabilities were almost completely paralyzed. Military industrial needs will naturally be affected, and exports will also be hit.

Overall, the total losses will probably exceed 500 million yen. Such a natural disaster cannot be said to be small. However, when we recall the Great Kanto Earthquake, the losses in major cities such as Tokyo and Yokohama were over 1 billion yen, accounting for one-tenth of Japan's national wealth. However, after five years, recovery was gradually seen. This wind disaster in Osaka is indeed very large, and the people have naturally suffered deeply, even to the point that it may affect Japan's overall national strength. However, there are several things in the midst of this that are worthy of our attention. First, the disaster relief measures of the Osaka City Government were extremely rapid. The activities of the police and the investigation of the disaster areas were unusually fast, and the accommodation of refugees was also very thorough. The city government immediately allocated 900,000 yuan for emergency expenses, which is something that should be done. Private donations for disaster relief were also significant. The Sumitomo financial group, with Sumitomo Kichizaemon, donated 1 million yuan for relief, which is already commendable. The Osaka Asahi Shimbun newspaper alone collected over 260,000 yuan in donations within three days. From this, we can see the enthusiasm of the Japanese people for disaster relief and the spirit of the entire country to overcome difficulties. Clenching their teeth and striving forward to overcome the forces of nature is indeed worthy of our attention. Looking westward at the motherland compatriots who are suffering many hardships, we should redouble our efforts! (September 24th, Osaka, Kita Ward)

American Journalist Group Discusses with Japanese Army Minister the Issue of Japanese Troops Stationed in Manchuria

American Journalists Believe it Contradicts the Independence of Manchukuo

Army Minister Hayashi Deems Withdrawal Impossible Under Current Conditions

The Nagoya Shimbun of Japan reported on the 23rd that Lowell Millett and ten other American journalists, after arriving in Tokyo, visited Army Minister Hayashi at 2:50 PM on the 22nd. They were translated by Motoyoshi Sada and spoke with Army Minister Hayashi for about an hour. The general situation was as follows: (1) American journalist Drummond asked, "The entire news group feels that the permanent stationing of Japanese troops in Manchuria greatly contradicts the independent nature of (Manchukuo)." Army Minister Hayashi replied, "The stationing of Japanese troops in Manchuria is due to the rampant banditry throughout Manchuria."

Page 11

"The Manchurian army does not yet have the ability to suppress them, and internal governance and national defense are not yet secure. Therefore, under the current conditions, the stationing of Japanese troops in Manchuria is necessary." (2) American journalist White asked, "According to your opinion, to what extent will Japanese troops need to be stationed in Manchuria in the future before they can withdraw?" Hayashi replied, "We will wait until the country is pacified and the Manchurian army is strong enough to resist foreign enemies. In my opinion, the training of the Manchurian army will still require a considerable period of time. The withdrawal of Japanese troops will be at least one or two years later." (3) White asked again, "Can the Japanese government not determine the time for the withdrawal of Japanese troops from Manchuria in advance?" Hayashi replied, "From the standpoint of joint defense by Japan and Manchuria, a unanimous opinion from both Japan and (Manchukuo) is required before a decision can be made."

Hebei Province War Zone Reorganization Problem

Reorganization Committee Can Be Established Soon

Difficulties Still Exist in Handling the Miyakoshi Case and Suppressing Bandits

Beiping Correspondence: Regarding the issue of the (war zone) reorganization, since the authorities decided to organize a (war zone) reorganization committee, the organization plan and the selection of committee members have been drafted by Huang Fu, the chairman of the Beiping Political Reorganization Committee. According to official sources, the establishment of the committee will be announced soon. The list of committee members will be announced by the Political Reorganization Committee in the form of an instruction. Although it is currently impossible to speculate on the exact number of members, it is a fact that representatives will be sent by seven organizations, including the Military Sub-Committee, the Political Reorganization Committee, the Hebei Provincial Government, the Luanyu District Public Office, the Jimi District Public Office, the Chahar Provincial Government, and the Beijing-Shenyang Railway Bureau.

As for the issue of the war zone, there are currently two matters that make the authorities unable to rest day and night: dealing with the Yutian Miyakoshi case and suppressing the bandits disturbing Yutian County. Regarding the former, although the truth about Miyakoshi's accidental killing has been jointly investigated by China and Japan, the Japanese side stated that it could not be compared with the Qian'an Fushan Temple incident, arguing that Miyakoshi was a comprador for the Japanese army stationed in Malanyu.

Regarding the latter, due to various practical considerations on our side, and the special circumstances of the so-called demilitarized zone, the suppression of bandits within the (war zone) is fraught with difficulties. The incident of the "Old Rat" occupying Funing County in the autumn of last year can serve as proof of how difficult it is for us to thoroughly suppress the bandits in Yutian today. This view can hardly be denied. Therefore, the authorities believe that, on the one hand, unfortunate incidents in the (war zone) should be prevented in the future, and on the other hand, the source of bandits in the (war zone) should be completely eliminated. This cannot be achieved without the early implementation of the (war zone) reorganization.

Huang Fu consulted with Li Zeyi last night (the 26th) and this morning (the 27th) on how to deal with the Miyakoshi case. By noon, a considerable decision had been made. Li left Beiping for Tianjin at around 4:00 p.m. that afternoon. It is understood that Li will begin negotiations with the Japanese side on this case. It is generally speculated that a satisfactory result can be obtained after a round of negotiations, and the situation will not escalate.

Regarding the issue of suppressing the Yutian bandits, the authorities have also made a decision. The first step is naturally to establish the (war zone) reorganization committee as soon as possible, so as to start implementing the reorganization. Once the (war zone) can be reorganized, it will not be difficult to suppress and eliminate the few hundred bandits. If the (war zone) can be reorganized smoothly, all disputes will naturally be reduced. Relevant parties have indicated that the Yutian Miyakoshi incident can be easily resolved, and the Yutian bandits can also be easily suppressed, provided that the Japanese side sincerely fulfills its promises and does not hinder our work in reorganizing the (war zone), so that the task can be accomplished successfully. (27th)

Bandit Alarm on the Border of Zunhua and Yutian in Hebei Province

Bandits Carry Heavy Firearms

Villages Are Burned and Killed Horribly

Tianjin Correspondence: The Hebei Provincial Government received telegrams today from Chen Baosheng, the magistrate of Yutian County, and Shen Zhongyu, the magistrate of Zunhua County, stating that at 3:00 p.m. on the 24th, a group of bandits, numbering about 300, crossed the border from Ji County into the border area of Yutian and Zunhua, occupying Daxiaolizhuang. They burned, killed, looted, and raped women. More than a dozen nearby villages were subjected to banditry. Villagers were confined and forbidden from leaving their homes. The bandits ordered them to point out where their valuables were. Some villagers risked their lives to escape to Zunhua County to report the incident. The magistrate, Shen Zhongyu, personally led the Third District Chief of the Security Team, Ma Jianchi, and the District Captain, Sun Ying, to assist Wang Zhanyuan's unit of the Third Battalion of the War Zone Security Force to encircle and suppress the bandits at 6:00 p.m. that day. At the same time, the Yutian County and Ji County militias also sent teams to block the bandits. At 7:00 p.m. that night, they began to engage the bandits. Because the bandits had two mortars, two mountain guns, several machine guns, and all kinds of large and small firearms, they resisted without retreating and threatened the national police with burning the entire village if they attacked. More than a thousand militiamen and police officers gathered and fought fiercely all night. By 7:00 a.m. on the 25th, the bandits could not hold out and retreated towards the Yanshan Pass. Wang Zhanyuan's security team immediately pursued them. According to another report from the Provincial Government, this group of bandits is still a secret unit secretly gathered by Shi Yousan and Liu Guitang. Therefore, their equipment is far from being as crude and uneven as that of ordinary bandits. The heavy firearms possessed by the bandits, in addition to the machine guns supplemented by Shi and Liu, the mortars and mountain guns were carried out during the mutiny of the puppet troops of Zhang Haipeng in Rehe. Shi and Liu lured them to join the bandit gang. The Provincial Government immediately telegraphed Ji, Zun, Qian, Yu, and Feng five counties to step up the search and suppression, in order to eliminate them.

Bandits with neat firearms were also found 20 li southeast of Funing County on the 24th. It is rumored that they were also former subordinates of Shi Yousan and Liu Guitang. Lou Yuying, the commander of the First Security Regiment, sent a team to search and suppress them, capturing their ringleader, Wang Mou, and more than a dozen accomplices. The rest of the bandits scattered and disappeared. In other counties in the war zone, many groups of bandits, claiming to be troops or brigades of a certain puppet unit, have also been found disturbing the area. The authorities are afraid that the bandit alarm incident of Qi Wenping, the "Old Rat," last year will happen again in eastern Hebei, so they secretly ordered the three security regiments compiled by the province and the militia book teams of various counties to strictly defend the territory. Yesterday, it was also heard that Liu Guitang and Shi Yousan secretly sent many people along the Beijing-Shenyang Railway line to set up puppet military offices everywhere for intelligence and liaison work. Their locations are all in foreign firms run by Japanese and Korean ruffians selling drugs. The authorities have ordered the responsible agencies in various places to secretly investigate and report, so as to prevent them. It is said that Shi Yousan is planning to go to Changchun with Kawashima Yoshiko and a certain Japanese person within a few days to make contact with the puppet organization. (25th)

Puppet Organizations in the Hebei War Zone

Government Cannot Interfere

Traitors Establish Branches

Beiping Correspondence: According to visitors from Tangshan, recently, reactionary elements, taking advantage of the special environment of the war zone, have recklessly opened up new fronts, organizing so-called puppet organizations such as the "Humanitarian Love Society" and the "Revive Manchuria Society," secretly engaging in activities and plotting wrongdoing. The so-called Humanitarian Love Society has its headquarters in a foreign concession in Tianjin, with branches in various parts of the war zone. Each branch has two directors. In Tangshan, it is called the Tangshan Second Branch of the North China Branch of the Humanitarian Love Society. The director, Sheng Guocai, and the deputy director, Liu Rudong, are secretly guided by the chairman of the Tangshan Residents' Association of a certain country, and are allocated funds. Members fill out application forms and are introduced by two or more people, pay a membership fee of two yuan, and are issued a wooden plaque and a copper badge each. If there is any illegal activity, the military police of a certain country will handle it with extraterritorial rights. Local government offices cannot directly intervene. Therefore, the society has developed very rapidly, and most of its members are lowlifes who do nothing good on weekdays. Among the traitors who have joined are Yao Mingshan, Liu Shaotang, Han Caizhang, Geng Zixiang, Cheng Yushan, Cui Zhen, Gao Junpeng, Gu Lanting, and more than ten others. The so-called Revive Manchuria Society is affiliated with the Love Society and is extremely secretive in its organization, containing the greatest political purpose. It is divided into three detachments in the war zone, all under the secret leadership of a certain country, and funds are allocated monthly by a certain country. It is said that the first detachment is stationed in Yuguan, with the detachment leader, Qi Longwu, recruiting party members and forming a uniform team of about 2,000 people, with 300 guns and 15,000 rounds of ammunition. The second detachment is stationed in Luan County, with the detachment leader, Han Shutian, having recruited about 3,000 traitors in Qian'an, Chengde, Laoting, Luan County, and other places, and has formed a plainclothes team of 2,000 people, with 400 guns and more than 20,000 rounds of ammunition. The third detachment is stationed in Tangshan, with its headquarters in Yutian, with the detachment leader, Zhao Dazhong, recruiting four to five thousand vagrants, obtaining 200 pistols and more than 10,000 rounds of ammunition, as well as 500 wooden fake guns. Although their current activities are very active, it is quite difficult for them to take action due to the strict precautions taken by the Hebei Security Team and local police militias, who are arresting them everywhere. (27th)

Confucius Clan in Qufu Plans to Publish "Qufu Series"

Jinan Correspondence: Recently, reports that the Japanese are persuading Kong Decheng, the Duke Yansheng of Qufu, to go to Japan have attracted attention from all parties. It is said that in recent years, the Japanese, Badie, have repeatedly persuaded Kong to go to Japan. This move did not start today and has been rejected. The Confucius clan will issue a declaration stating that they will never participate in the Japanese Confucius ritual. Furthermore, the Confucius clan plans to publish the "Qufu Series" and asks the government to reorganize the Confucius sacrificial fields, which are now underway. The details are as follows: Japanese Persuade Kong Decheng to Go to Japan

Recent reports stated that the Japanese plan to persuade Kong Decheng, the Duke Yansheng of Qufu, and his uncle, Kong Lingcan, to go to Japan to participate in the spring ceremony. The Confucius clan has already stated that they will definitely not participate. It is said that the instigation of this matter did not start today. After the September 18th Incident, in addition to swallowing our Northeast, a certain Japanese person went to Qufu to persuade Kong Decheng to go to Japan, saying that Japan has always respected Confucius, that the Confucius Temple in Tokyo is being extensively repaired, and that a Confucius ceremony will be held next spring. He invited him to go east to participate and offered generous treatment. The Confucius clan replied that Confucius's way is universal and does not distinguish between national boundaries. While they are grateful that your country respects Confucius, given the recent relationship between China and Japan, it is really inconvenient to go. They politely declined. Afterwards, anyone who went there was not received. Recently, the Japanese Toyota requested an audience and was also rejected. Also, on Confucius's birthday this year, representatives from the National Government and the Provincial Government went to Qufu to pay their respects. Six Japanese people requested to participate in the ceremony. The Confucius Mansion replied that your country can come to visit, but it would be difficult to comply if you participate in the ceremony at the same time as the government representatives. The Japanese people left in dismay. Their various methods are like this, and it is not known what other tricks will appear in the future.

Kong Decheng Denies Going to Japan

Kong Decheng, the Duke Yansheng, and his clan members published an announcement in the newspapers in Jinan, stating that they would never go to Japan. The original text is as follows: (The New Tianjin News of September 22 and the Yongbao of the same day reported that the Tokyo United Telegram of the 21st stated that the newly renovated Confucius Temple in Japan will be completed and a commemorative meeting will be held in April next year, inviting Kong Decheng, the 77th generation descendant of Confucius, and his uncle, Kong Lingcan, to participate. Decheng was very surprised after reading it. Decheng and his uncle, Kong Lingcan, had never heard of this matter. If there is an invitation at that time, Decheng and the members of our clan will definitely not participate. We hereby publish this statement. Kong Decheng and the members of the Kong clan jointly announce.)

Plans to Publish the Qufu Series

After the Confucius birthday ceremony in Qufu this year, the Confucius clan sent representatives to Jinan to express their gratitude and to discuss the renovation of the Confucius Temple and the publication of books. The Confucius Mansion in Qufu has many books, some of which have been published and are not widely circulated and need to be reprinted, and some of which have not yet been engraved. The Confucius clan intends to compile and publish them all at once to spread them widely, naming it the "Qufu Series." However, due to the lack of capital, they plan to ask the government to lend them some money first, sell the books, and then repay the loan. The Provincial Government is very concerned about preserving ancient books and may approve it in the future. There are many kinds of series. As far as we know, there are Kong Jihan, whose courtesy name is Honggu, "The Writings of the Weiboshe" and the unpublished manuscripts of Weiboshe (Kong lived during the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty and was contemporary with Dai Dongyuan. There is also the Weiboshe Series, which is printed together with Dai's posthumous writings, with Dai's books on one side and Kong's books on the other). His books mainly discuss elementary learning and are highly valued at home and abroad and are the most valuable. The plates are well preserved. There is also Ruan Yuan's "Examination of Metal and Stone Illustrations" (Ruan was an educational inspector in Shandong during the Daoguang period of the Qing Dynasty). Because Ruan and Kong were related by marriage, the plates are stored in Qufu (the plates are not in the Confucius Mansion but are known to be stored in the home of a Confucius clan member, and further investigation is needed). Kong Guanglin, whose courtesy name is Congbai, wrote "Kong's Explanation of Classics" (the plates are stored in the library). There are also three kinds of lyrics and songs, Kong Chuanzhi and Kong Chuanduo, the Duke Yansheng, wrote books such as music scores. In addition, there is "The History of Literature in Que Li," "Confucius Family Rituals" (recording the ancient wedding and funeral customs of the Confucius family in great detail), "A Broad Record of the Ancestral Court," etc. ("A Broad Record of the Ancestral Court" was originally a book recording the anecdotes of the temple court of the Confucius family, but it is now circulating in the market as "A Broad Record of the Temple Court"). Kong Guangsen, whose courtesy name is Zhixuan, was the younger brother of Kong Guanglin, and wrote ("The Writings of Zhixuan"), which includes "A General Explanation of Gongyang," "A Commentary on the Great Dai Ritual," and "The Yizhen Hall Collection," respecting Zheng Kangcheng and explaining the meaning of the classics. There are also "The Collection of Poetry Sounds and Examples of Poetry Sounds," etc. The above books are just a small part of the many books, which may be rarely circulated in the world or have never been printed, and are of great value for widespread circulation.

Reorganize the Confucius Sacrificial Fields in Qufu

The Confucius Mansion in Qufu originally had 4,000 qing of sacrificial fields. Over time, much of the land was in Nanyang Lake. In recent years, due to changes in rivers and lakes, some of the land has rolled into the lake. There is also a lot of land in Fengpei, Xiao, and Dang counties in Jiangsu Province, which is boundless and without boundary stones. Over time, it has been impossible to verify, and much of it has been encroached upon by others. Representatives of the Confucius Mansion stated to the representatives of the National Government and the Provincial Government the recent economic difficulties of the Confucius Mansion and asked for the reorganization of the sacrificial fields. Now, Han Fuju, the main administrator of the Provincial Government, has ordered Kong Decheng to submit a detailed register of the land for review and reorganization, and to revere the sacrificial rites.

Restoring the Confucius Temple Requires 500,000

The Provincial Government is currently sending personnel to survey and estimate the cost of repairing the Confucius Temple (and preparing construction funds. It is said that the renovation of the Dacheng Hall requires 100,000 yuan, the renovation of the two corridors requires 100,000 yuan, and the Kuiwen Pavilion also requires 60,000 yuan, totaling about 500,000 yuan. If the county government can raise more funds and carry out extensive renovations, making it more solid and magnificent, it would be a grand event.

The defense groups of Songjiang, Fengxian, and Qingpu counties are now ordered by the Provincial Security Department to be reorganized into the 12th Battalion of the Jiangsu Provincial Security Team. The water patrol Second and Third Companies will be reorganized with Qingpu, with the company headquarters in Qingpu, divided into platoons one, two, and three. The first platoon will be organized by Qingpu, the remaining team soldiers of the Song Police Team will be merged into the second platoon, and Fengxian will be organized into the third platoon. The reorganization is currently underway.

In June of this year, a pirate gang robbed official salt outside Wusongkou, losing more than 1,800 dans. Recently, he received a secret report that Wu Changyou, a key suspect in the case, was hiding in the Changtai area. He immediately dispatched officers and informants to secretly follow him for many days. Because Wu was strong and powerful, they did not dare to act rashly. On the morning of the day before yesterday, Wu was drinking tea at the Wanchun Garden Teahouse in the city. The officers reported to the County Public Security Bureau, requesting police assistance. The bureau dispatched many police officers to encircle and arrest him, nearly allowing him to escape. Fortunately, the police officers bravely stepped forward and captured him. It is said that Wu is a native of Yuyao, Zhejiang, and is nearly 50 years old.

A Disturbance Caused by Spectators at the Huaqin Opera

A Huaqin opera troupe has recently arrived in the Shisi'an area of this county and has been performing for nearly a week, with full houses day and night. For the purpose of alleviating poverty among the poor, Wu, the district head of the First District of the city, plans to establish loan offices for the poor both inside and outside the city. The matter was proposed at the district affairs meeting yesterday and passed, deciding to set up eight locations outside Loumen, outside Liumen, outside Xumen, outside Fengmen, outside Qimen, in Zheyu Lane, in Daping Lane, and in the East Central Market. Monk Found in Tianfu Nunnery

Deqing, the abbess of the Tianfu Nunnery at No. 5 Cao'an Lane, Guanqian Street, Suzhou City, is 44 years old. In the spring of last year, she went to Putuo to offer incense and met Tongzhao, the abbot of Putuo Temple, and they had a physical relationship. In the summer, Deqing returned to Suzhou. In the spring of this year, Tongzhao came to Suzhou from Ningbo and stayed at the Tianfu Nunnery, where he smoked red pills and opium. However, his actions were very secretive, and few outsiders knew about it. Someone reported it to the Second Public Security Bureau, which sent Inspector Cui and police officers to search the nunnery on the 27th. They arrested the nun, Deqing, and the monk, Tongzhao, and seized smoking paraphernalia on the spot. Jiading

Ancient Tomb of the Yuan Dynasty Discovered

Xu Wenbiao, of South Main Street in this city, purchased more than ten mu of land from the Wang family in front of the County Junior High School in North Gate, built a surrounding wall and fence, and built a new house inside. While digging the ground, he discovered an ancient tomb. It was very deep, covered with huge stone slabs, and surrounded by brick walls, making it extremely strong. There were five coffins in the tomb, as well as jade ruyi, vases, porcelain bowls, tiles, and other funerary objects. There was also a lot of mercury scattered in the tomb. There were several stone tablets, but the characters were eroded and difficult to recognize. Among them were words such as "Chen Shi'an of X, returned to the Xu family from XX, September 26th of the fourteenth year of Zhizheng," which can be known to have been built in the fourteenth year of Emperor Shun of the Yuan Dynasty, 600 years ago.

Comply with the Urban Land Price Declaration

Qian Sunqing and Li Tipping, members of the County Land Price Declaration Assistance Committee, convened a discussion meeting yesterday at the County Chamber of Commerce for the purpose of promoting the declaration of urban land prices. Town chiefs and local figures from the urban area attended the meeting. The representatives spoke one after another and discussed for two hours before reaching a decision. Regarding the issue of land price declaration, it is a matter of legal decree and should be complied with. However, the collection of land price tax and land price appreciation tax should be postponed during this time of economic depression. Only when the economy actually turns around can we carefully consider ways to ease the burden on the people. As for the standard for declaring land prices, the town chiefs should first conduct a detailed investigation of the actual situation in all aspects, and then discuss and determine it at another meeting on the fifth of next month.

Chief of the Second Sub-bureau Accused of Illegal Conduct

Gao Lian (native of Chongshan County), the chief of the Second Public Security Sub-bureau outside Guangfu Gate, severely injured the ankle of Tan Genquan, the son of Tan Fengshi, a resident of Nianshang Lane, on the evening of the 16th of this month. Traitorous Merchants Smuggling Grain for Export Blocked

Li Youxiang, the owner of the Yishengchang firm in Lingdian Port, the Fourth District, has been buying at low prices and smuggling grain for export every year during the new wheat harvest, in order to make huge profits. This autumn, the miscellaneous grains harvest was poor, and there was a famine. Families of Victims Request Detention of Baohua Steamer

Letter from Lawyer Shen Qi

Dear Sir, According to Dai Hanyun, I'm writing to you regarding a piece of news from Chuansha published in the Shenbao on the 20th of this month. The news stated that Huang Dechang and other farmer representatives from Hengsha County filed a criminal lawsuit with the Chuansha County Government against the Nanjingsha Affairs Bureau and the Education Public Group, accusing them of extracting rent director Dai Hanyun's name and exploiting the people for their own selfish gain, neglecting their duties, and causing a great disaster last year. Dai Hanyun passed the responsibility onto his superiors, claiming that although the difference fee had been ordered to stop being collected in the 18th year, the Nanjingsha School still ordered it to be collected. All the money collected over the years was turned over, 40% was used to repair the embankment, and the tenants were responsible, which was not a personal decision. The Nanjingsha School Board and the Education Public Group officials all had far reaching means, but the Chuansha County Government actually ruled the criminal charges as not guilty and ordered a separate civil lawsuit to be filed. The representatives were not satisfied with the ruling and filed an appeal, etc. This is not in accordance with the facts. When Huang Dechang sued Hanyun, he filed the lawsuit as a plaintiff and did not state that he was a representative of such-and-such. The difference fee was not ordered to stop being collected. All the fees collected by Hanyun during his tenure were reported, and there are register books to prove it. Even last year, the Sixth District Office sent a letter requesting that the difference fee be allocated to epidemic prevention expenses, and the payment was made after reporting to the Nanpu School Board and receiving approval. There are also correspondence documents that can be checked. Last year, the cost of raising the Shunli embankment was to be shared by the Nanjingsha School and the tenants, but because the tenants did not agree, Hanyun notified accountant Yuan Baiyan to wait for the merchants and tenants to discuss the matter before distributing the money. There is also the original letter to prove it. Hanyun has been in Sha for five years and only knows to be dutiful and abide by the law, disregarding personal interests. There is no need for the Nanjingsha School and the Education Public Group to use means in order to protect him. Now, the case has been ruled by the Shanghai District Court, which rejected the appeal of Huang Dechang and others. The truth will be revealed. However, the news falsely accuses Hanyun of extracting rent director's name and exploiting the people for their own selfish gain and neglecting their duties, and that the Nanjingsha School Board and the Education Public Group officials had far reaching means, which is related to the reputation of Hanyun and others. Please represent us and send a letter requesting a correction from your newspaper. Sincerely, Lawyer Shen Qi, 23.9.28
