Local News

The Chinese Red Cross Convention Closes Yesterday

A board of directors was elected yesterday, and a photograph was taken to commemorate Mr. Liu.

A declaration was issued, reporting the significance of convening the convention.

The National Convention of the Chinese Red Cross continued to be held at the City Chamber of Commerce yesterday. The convention followed the detailed regulations, revised the general and branch bylaws, and began elections at 5:30 PM, with the results announced late at night. The details are recorded below:

Revision of Bylaws

Those present yesterday included more than two hundred representatives from the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of the Navy, and various provincial branches. The chairmen, Wen Lanting, Guan Jiongzhi, Wang Peiyuan, and Lin Kanghou, reported on the minutes of the fourth meeting. The convention then discussed and revised the general and branch bylaws according to the detailed regulations. Guan Jiongzhi read the revisions article by article, and they were passed. At 5:30 PM, the election of directors and supervisors began. Liu Mengyang, Ji Heqin, Dong Xinqin, and Wang Kuibi were publicly nominated as ballot counters; Ling Guyu, Zhou Guangjiu, Yan Yicen, and He Jingzhai were nominated as ballot collectors; and Zhu Dingyi, Zhang Liangbi, Li Yingnan, and Wang Peiyuan were nominated as ballot supervisors. After the election, the convention declaration was read, and the convention was adjourned.

Elected Directors

The list of elected directors for the first board of directors of the Chinese Red Cross is as follows: Lin Kanghou, Wang Peiyuan, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Guan Jiongzhi, Wen Lanting, Du Yuesheng, Wang Yiting, Wang Zhengting, Zhu Ziqiao, Yan Huiqing, Xu Shiying, Shi Liangcai, Wang Zhenchuan, and Liu Hongsheng. The following fifteen individuals were elected as directors. Huang Hanzhi, Yao Yuqin, Gu Zhuxuan, Li Yingnan, Zhang Xiantai, Qian Xinzhi, and Zhu Yinjiang were elected as alternate directors.

Convention Declaration

The instability of the world situation has never been greater than it is today. Looking back sixteen years to the European War, it ended with the world's expectation of peace. The League of Nations was born from the world's expectation of peace. All the countries that directly participated in the war have their own regrets. Those who were indirectly affected by the war without participating in it also realized that the war was too inhumane. Therefore, the discussion of stopping wars and reducing troops also arose. For a time, the atmosphere of peace permeated the world. This can truly be called the good fortune of mankind and the gospel of the world. However, not long after, new conflicts of interest gradually emerged between countries, creating an unstable situation. Although countries still outwardly promoted the movement for peace, they secretly expanded their military preparations. Consequently, some observers of the situation suddenly published a prediction that a second world war would occur in 1936. Those who had hoped for peace became discouraged, and then the September 18th Incident in Northeast China suddenly occurred, shocking the world and leading people to believe that it was a sign of the Second World War. Countries then began to prepare for war, revealing their false masks of peace and intensifying their competition to expand their military armaments. In this case, even if the Second World War does not occur in 1936, it will ultimately only be a matter of time. Our country, as a weak nation, is caught in the middle. If we unfortunately encounter this change, how can we cope? Can we bear to sit idly by while our regions are devastated and our soldiers and civilians are killed and injured without thinking of how to rescue them? At this time, the only thing that can preserve our country's position in the international community is our Red Cross Society. Our country's Red Cross Society was founded in the 30th year of the Guangxu reign of the late Qing Dynasty. In the 33rd year of the Guangxu reign, it formed an alliance with the International Red Cross Society and was included in the international community, obtaining recognition from the allied countries. Since then, it has experienced the domestic revolutionary wars and the civil wars in various provinces, and has provided relief to the natural disasters in countries such as Japan, the United States, and Russia. It has also responded to incidents such as the September 18th Incident and the January 28th Incident. For thirty years, the general and branch societies have been almost constantly prepared to rescue and protect civilian casualties. In times of peace, it has also been constantly engaged in disaster relief, epidemic prevention, and assisting neighboring countries with their disasters. What cannot be avoided is that the Red Cross Society is a new undertaking in our country, and people's understanding is still not genuine. Therefore, there are not many members, and resources are weak. All kinds of undertakings are ultimately unavoidable to be beyond our capabilities. This can be barely coped with in ordinary times. However, at a time when the atmosphere of the Second World War is pervasive, if we continue to make do with what we have without thinking of how to improve, if we encounter a major change that is even more severe than the European War, the areas of North China and the Southeast coast may fall into an indescribable state, and even the major commercial ports of the country may be difficult to protect. With such a small scale and incomplete equipment of the Red Cross Society, how can it fulfill its heavenly duty of universal love, compassion for soldiers, and rescuing those in distress? This is in terms of responding to the changes of the times. From the perspective of the association itself, the association was established at the end of the late Qing Dynasty. All organizations have been following the same system for thirty years. Times have changed, and it is urgent to make changes in order to meet the needs of the times. All of this is the reason for convening this national member representative convention. This convention was held on September 24, the 23rd year of the Republic of China, and closed on September 28. In addition to the representatives of the general association members, there were more than one hundred branches in various provinces with more than two hundred representatives. The proposals made were also able to meet the needs and were able to express the spirit of striving for improvement. From now on, the association will have a new look and open a new era. This is a congratulation to the future of the association. To summarize the important cases decided by this convention, the outline is recorded as follows: (1) In accordance with the Regulations for the Management of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China promulgated by the National Government and the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the Regulations for the Management of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China promulgated by the Executive Yuan, the bylaws of the general and branch associations of the association shall be amended to ensure that the organization is complete and to improve the efficiency of handling affairs. (2) Reduce membership dues, recruit more youth members, establish a women's department, and train rescue and nursing personnel, and pre-store rescue materials, so that the internal affairs can be enriched at ordinary times, and it can be responded to with ease in the event of a change. (3) Establish well-equipped hospitals in the capital and various ports, and set up disaster relief and relief agencies, so that it can treat the diseases of civilians and save the suffering of the poor at ordinary times, and can treat Chinese and foreign wounded soldiers in the event of a change, so as to respect humanity, so as not to temporarily establish new ones and the effectiveness is insufficient. The above is just a brief overview of the major ones. There are many other cases decided, which cannot be listed one by one. Here, a solemn announcement is made to the members of the general and branch associations that the cases decided this time must be implemented, so that the organization of the general and branch associations themselves is sound, and the response to peacetime and wartime will be effective. It must be known that the period of international peace is far away. No matter what our country's attitude is at that time, its position will be extremely dangerous. All members of our Red Cross have no power to reverse this disaster, but only have the great wish to work hard and serve the association, with the idea of loving and saving people, in order to win the sympathy of the people of the country and the international community. In peacetime, they should also work hard to help the poor and relieve disasters, directly creating welfare for the society and indirectly creating welfare for themselves. Now, in order to arouse the common attention of the comrades of the association and the people of the whole country, this declaration is made.

Song Ziwen Talks About Unified Water Conservancy

Establish a National Water Conservancy Commission

Appoint Kong Xiangxi as Chairman, with an annual budget of six million

Kong Xiangrong, Li Yizhi, and others as Standing Committee Members

According to the Central News Agency, Mr. Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the National Economic Council, entered Beijing on the 25th to attend the standing committee meeting of the National Economic Council. He completed his official duties and took a special express train from Beijing to Shanghai at 5:00 PM on the 27th, arriving in Shanghai at 11:30 PM. On the morning of the 28th, he met with reporters from various newspapers at his private residence on Avenue Road and made the following remarks:

Unified Water Conservancy

Mr. Song first mentioned that the most important resolution of the Standing Committee of the National Economic Council, which was convened in Beijing this time, was the unified national water conservancy plan. It was decided to establish a National Water Conservancy Commission under the National Economic Council. The chairman will be Minister Kong, and two other standing committee members will be appointed. One of the candidates is Kong Xiangrong, director of the labor relief group of the Yellow River Flood Relief Committee, and the other is Li Yizhi, chairman of the Yellow River Water Conservancy Commission. As for the unified water conservancy plan, it will be carried out according to the decision of the Central Political Conference, so that national water conservancy can be unified. The budget will be 500,000 yuan per month from the Ministry of Finance, with an annual budget of 6 million yuan. After the establishment of the Water Conservancy Commission, it will become an affiliated agency of the National Economic Council.

Wei River Loan

As for the Wei River loan, Yang Hucheng, director of pacification in Shaanxi, came to Shanghai last month to negotiate with the banking community and agreed to borrow 1.55 million yuan. The detailed procedures have been agreed upon, and Mr. Yang will send someone to Shanghai to sign the loan contract. The collateral for the loan is (1) the water field tax (referring to the water field tax on both sides of the Wei, Jing, and Luo canals) and (2) the provincial business tax revenue. Mr. Song believes that this loan and repayment method is appropriate, because borrowing for construction means repaying the loan from the income of the constructed project, which is indeed a win-win situation.

Next Year's Funding

Most of the funding for the National Economic Council next year has not yet been secured, so this time, the Standing Committee decided to assign Minister Kong and himself to be responsible for planning. He and others will immediately start planning according to this decision, so that the work of the National Economic Council will not be slightly frustrated due to lack of economic resources.

Technical Cooperation

The technical cooperation between the National Economic Council and the League of Nations is still actively continuing. Dr. Raciman, the technical liaison officer previously sent to China by the League of Nations, has completed his term and returned to Geneva. Therefore, the League of Nations has now decided to send Dr. Robeit Haas to continue to serve in this position. Mr. Haas is the Minister of Transportation of the League of Nations, and was the Secretary-General of the Lytton Investigation Team organized by the League of Nations. When Dr. Raciman had not yet arrived in China, the League of Nations had decided to send Mr. Haas to China. Later, Mr. Haas served as the Secretary-General of the Lytton Investigation Team, so Raciman was sent instead. Now that Mr. Ra's term has expired, Mr. Haas has been sent to China, and is expected to arrive in China within one or two months. Several water conservancy experts will also come to China with Mr. Haas. As for Mr. Haas's salary, it will be borne by the League of Nations.

Improved Silk

Dr. Mari, a silk expert specially sent to China by the League of Nations, completed his term in January of this year, so he was reappointed for another year. Since arriving in China, Mr. Ma has visited Sichuan, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Guangdong, and other provinces to investigate the silk situation. Now he has researched the method of combining Jiangsu and Zhejiang silkworm species with Italian silkworm species in Hangzhou. After obtaining considerable results, it is decided to first test it in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, and then promote it to the silkworm breeding provinces across the country.

Answers to Reporters' Questions

Mr. Song finally answered questions from various reporters: (1) Regarding the inaccurate rumors of US Senator Nye, he only saw it in the newspaper. (2) The Fifth National Congress decided to be held as scheduled, and he decided to go to Beijing to attend, but there were no proposals. (3) The rumor that Dr. Yan Huiqing, the ambassador to the Soviet Union, has requested to resign due to his old age and physical weakness has also only been seen in newspapers. (4) It is rumored that the Central Committee will send Central Committee members Huang Shaoxiong and Zhang Puquan to Hong Kong and Guangdong to consult with the Central Committee members in Guangdong about the Fifth National Congress. It was not mentioned in Beijing, and it is feared that it is not confirmed.

The negotiation process for this matter has been going on for a long time. At that time, our country was conducting negotiations with countries such as the United Kingdom, France, Italy, and Japan at the same time. However, each country shirked responsibility. Only the Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, through the efforts of the former Italian envoy to China, Qi Yanuojue, and various important figures in our country's diplomatic circles, finally succeeded in exchanging documents on the 26th of this month. All other related countries were greatly surprised when they heard about it. According to comments from relevant diplomatic figures, Italy's move further demonstrates Mussolini's decisive spirit of acting independently. It is expected that Germany and the United Kingdom will follow Italy's lead and exchange ambassadors with China. Germany has no special rights and interests in China, and British diplomacy has always been smooth, so it should not lag behind again in this move.

Ambassadorial Candidates It is internally decided that the first Chinese ambassador to Italy will be Liu Wendao, the current Chinese envoy to Italy. It is also internally decided that the first Italian ambassador to China will be Bascari, the current Italian envoy to China. Envoy Liu is scheduled to attend the Fifth National Congress and then take the letter of credence to Italy to formally meet with the Italian Emperor and present it. The Italian envoy will wait for the formal appointment and the letter of credence to be sent to Shanghai before going to Beijing to meet with Chairman Lin and present the letter of credence.

Envoy Liu Expresses According to what Liu Wendao told visiting reporters yesterday, China is the birthplace of Eastern civilization, while Italy is the birthplace of European civilization. The elevation of the envoys of China and Italy to ambassadors will make a great contribution to the increase of diplomatic relations between China and Italy, the communication of Eastern and Western cultures, and the protection of world peace. He feels very happy about this. According to international practice, the status of an ambassador is much higher than that of an envoy. The ambassador can visit the foreign minister of the host country at any time, and can meet with the head of state once every three days when necessary. He can also invite the head of state of the host country to participate in various social interactions at any time. All of these can be used to increase the diplomatic relations between the two countries and provide great convenience and benefit in diplomacy.

Italian Envoy Speaks Italian Envoy Bascari said that the event of the elevation of the envoys of China and Italy has now been officially confirmed. He has very good feelings about the implementation of the elevation of the envoys of China and Italy. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has always regarded the communication between Europe and Asia as his own responsibility. You should remember the speech given by the Italian Prime Minister at the Asian Student Conference held in Rome in December last year. This time, the implementation of the elevation of the envoys of China and Italy will be of great benefit to the diplomatic relations between China and Italy. In the future, the economic, political, and cultural relations between China and Italy will definitely become closer. As for whether the Italian embassy in China will be moved to Beijing in the future, or will remain in Shanghai, he cannot tell, because the candidate for the Italian ambassador to China has not yet been announced. Embassy Address However, according to reliable information from diplomatic circles, the Italian embassy in China will currently be located at the old site of the Italian envoy to China on Jing'an Temple Road. In the future, it will be moved to Nanjing, but the issue of moving to Beijing cannot be realized in the short term.

Finance Minister Kong Hosts Liu Finance Minister Kong Xiangxi and his wife specially hosted Liu Wendao, the Chinese envoy to Italy, and his wife at their residence on West Avenue Road at 7:00 PM last night to celebrate the success of the elevation of the envoys of China and Italy. Song Ziwen, Wu Tiecheng, and other important figures were also invited to accompany them. The party ended happily at about 10:00 PM.

The duration of this trip is tentatively set at one year. After returning to China, he will report the investigation results to the government for reference. The China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau Ceases Operation

The Shanghai Preparatory Office has been dismantled.

Central Government to establish a separate entity.

The China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau, championed by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, had established a preparatory office in Shanghai and was actively progressing. It is now understood that the Bureau's preparations have ceased. The Central Government will instead organize a National Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau. All previously collected provincial share capital will be returned in full to the respective provinces and cities. It is understood that the capital amount has been decided to increase to four million yuan, which will be initially borrowed from the Central Bank. The detailed circumstances before and after are recorded as follows:

A Batch of Telegrams

(1) A telegram from Gu Xin-yi, Director of the Preparatory Office of the China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau, to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek stated: "The Provisional Meeting of the Executive Yuan has resolved to establish a Grain Bureau under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Finance as soon as possible." Therefore, the preparatory work of this office should cease immediately. The share capital previously collected from the provinces should also be returned in full to clear procedures. (2) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed the Executive Yuan, stating: "Since the establishment of the Preparatory Office of the China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau, repeated telegrams have urged provincial and municipal governments to submit their share capital on file. Now that the Executive Yuan has resolved that the government should establish and manage the Bureau under the Ministry of Finance, the Director and others have requested to cease preparatory work, in accordance with the division of authority, and to return the share capital already paid by the provinces and cities in order to conclude matters. This should be approved. In addition to instructing compliance, please expedite the establishment of the Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau by the Ministry of Finance."

Reasons for Reorganization

The motivation for establishing the China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau stemmed from the representatives of eight provinces seeking to alleviate rural distress and develop the grain business. In November of last year, a preparatory office was established in Shanghai, with Preparatory Director Gu Xin-yi responsible for its progress. The share capital was determined to be two million yuan, to be borne equally by official and commercial parties, with the aim of collecting shares before January of this year. However, until last month, grain merchants from various provinces had not yet fully paid, causing delays in its establishment. During the provisional meeting of the Executive Yuan the previous month, it was also noted that the drought in various regions was severe, necessitating the urgent establishment of a Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau to provide relief and stabilize market prices. It was resolved to dismantle the already-in-preparation China Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau and instruct the Ministry of Finance to establish a separate entity to expedite its realization.

The Ministry of Finance Takes Charge

After receiving the telegram from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi also believed that, in the face of rural bankruptcy, the Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau was indeed necessary to be expanded to provide relief. The previous Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau's official capital of only one million yuan was insufficient for the task. Now that it has been reorganized to be established by the government, it is proposed to increase the capital to four million yuan, and at the same time expand the organization, establishing grain transportation and sales bureau branches in various regions, and establishing new-style rural warehouses universally. In years of abundant harvests, when there is overproduction, the grain can be purchased and stored in warehouses, preventing low grain prices from harming farmers. If there is a drought like this year, with poor harvests for farming families, the warehouses can release surplus rice to regulate the market. This would stabilize market prices and prevent unscrupulous merchants from monopolizing the market again.

Urgent Establishment

In order to expedite its establishment, Kong Xiangxi has instructed the recently established preparatory office in Beijing to intensify its work and actively proceed. According to a report by the China Eastern News Agency reporter yesterday, preparatory matters have largely been completed, and personnel have been dispatched to Hunan, Hubei, and Anhui to investigate the actual situation. In order to prevent disasters in various regions, special commissioners have been separately dispatched to important rice-producing areas such as Hankou and Changsha to oversee the construction of storage warehouses. The internal organization and staff of the Bureau have also been internally determined, and all expenses have been approved. Once established, the Central Bank will initially provide loans.

Cases of Violating Stamp Tax Laws to be Handled by Judicial Organs

Order from the Ministry of Judicial Administration to all Courts to comply.

To be implemented starting November 1st.

The Ministry of Judicial Administration has decreed that, starting from November 1st, cases of violating stamp tax laws will be handled by judicial organs. Special orders have been given to the High Courts of all provinces to comply. The original text is recorded as follows: "As approved by the Ministry of Finance, cases of violating stamp tax laws, except for the Shanghai Concession area which is handled by the Shanghai Special District Court, the remaining inland areas are handled by the stamp tax branch bureaus. However, the penalties imposed by these branch bureaus are often inappropriate, resulting in innocent merchants being unfairly penalized. Although the review is more fair in places where committees for reviewing cases of violating stamp tax regulations have been established, due to the different situations in each location, they cannot be universally established, which has a significant impact on the future of tax administration. In order to thoroughly reform stamp tax matters in accordance with the resolutions of the current financial conference, this Ministry has ordered all provincial stamp tax collection agencies to uniformly close down by the end of October of this year. New stamp tax stamps with a pagoda design, manufactured by this Ministry, have been agreed upon with the Ministry of Communications, and starting from November 1st, they will be entrusted to post offices in all provinces to sell on commission. The inspection of stamp tax matters will be the responsibility of the provincial, municipal, and county governments, with personnel dispatched by the provincial stamp tax and alcohol bureaus to conduct random checks at any time, and personnel dispatched by this Ministry to supervise progress. Hereafter, cases of violating stamp tax regulations that are discovered must not be unilaterally penalized by inspection agencies in order to eliminate longstanding malpractices. It is proposed to follow the precedent of the Shanghai Special District Court handling cases of violating stamp tax, and uniformly submit them to the judicial organs in various regions for handling. The judicial organs of your esteemed offices should be instructed to instruct the subordinate courts and county governments concurrently handling judicial affairs to comply. Starting from November 1st of this year, cases of violating stamp tax regulations submitted for trial by various cities and counties should be handled in accordance with the revised Rules for Judicial Organs to Impose Penalties and Execute the Provisional Stamp Tax Regulations. In addition to submitting reports and issuing separate orders for announcements, a corresponding notification should be made for examination and implementation. This order is issued for compliance and for informing subordinates to comply."

The Haining Relief Association Publishes Statistics on Drought Losses

Crop losses valued at over 7 million

More than 150,000 people cannot survive without relief

The Haining Drought Relief Association, located on the third floor of the Gong De Lin on Park Road, yesterday received a formal report from the Haining County Government on the drought statistics for the county. The figures are as follows: (1) Rice affected: 386,272 mu; (2) Sugarcane affected: 11,501 mu; (3) Taro affected: 5,987 mu; (4) Soybeans affected: 178,460 mu; (5) Yuan Shen affected: 90 mu; (6) Cotton affected: 19,504 mu; (7) Watermelons affected: 577 mu; (8) Snow pears affected: 138 mu; (9) Cabbage affected: 1,500 mu; (10) Pumpkins affected: 227 mu; (11) Sweet potatoes affected: 114 mu; (12) Hemp affected: 8,090 mu; (13) Chrysanthemums affected: 1,431 mu; (14) Mulberry seedlings affected: 159 mu; (15) Mulberry leaves affected: 133,491 mu. The total affected area is over 757,545 mu, while the total area of the county is only over 758,951 mu. The total population of the county is 364,094, and the number of people affected by the disaster is 317,800, of which one-half cannot survive without relief. The value of crop losses due to the drought, calculated at the lowest estimate, is also worth 7,888,293 yuan.

Ya Tax in Zhabei, Wusong, and Other Districts Consolidated under Municipal Management

All taxes must be paid and verified by today

Since the Zhabei, Wusong, Jiangwan, and Yinhang districts, formerly under the jurisdiction of Baoshan County, were placed under the administration of Shanghai Municipality, the ya tax certificates for businesses in these districts have continued to be issued by Baoshan County. In order to standardize the ya certificates in Shanghai Municipality, they have been consolidated under the management of the Municipal Finance Bureau. Therefore, businesses in these districts with old ya certificates must submit them to the Zhabei Inspection Office of the Municipal Finance Bureau at the intersection of Zhabei and Xinjiang Roads by the end of this month for verification. As the 30th of this month is a Sunday, today (the 29th) is the last day. Businesses that fail to submit their certificates for verification by the deadline will have their old ya certificates invalidated. Therefore, businesses in these districts holding ya certificates issued by Baoshan County must take note.

Son's illness, mother's death, one misfortune after another.

The two of them lived together in a thatched shed near the Dahyang Bridge in Zhabei, enduring hardship. Unfortunately, Ms. Zhao and her son had terrible luck. Recently, Yuqing fell ill and was bedridden. Ms. Zhao sought medical treatment for him. Ms. Zhao had been losing sleep for days due to her son's illness, making her mentally and physically exhausted. She wanted to avoid it, but it was already too late. Selling Dead Crabs Leads to Fatal Assault

Yu Guilin Sentenced to Four Years and Eight Months

Yu Guilin, a crab vendor from Minhang, 34 years old, transported crabs to Shanghai on the morning of the 18th of this month and offered them for sale at the Yongtai Fish Shop at No. 6, Xiaodongmen Street, French Concession. Zhou Heshang, a vendor from Haining residing at No. 103, Huanghe Road, French Concession, purchased crabs from Yu. When Zhou wanted to remove the dead crabs, Yu refused, and the two began to argue. Yu became violent, striking Zhou's left chest below the heart with a punch. Zhou immediately collapsed to the ground, unable to get up, due to the injury to his lung. The police arrived and took Yu into custody. Zhou was sent to Guangci Hospital, but died before he could be treated. The body was transported to the morgue for inspection. The Second Special Court dispatched personnel to verify the cause of death, and the family collected the body. The police sent Yu Guilin to the Second Special Court, which prosecuted him for negligent homicide. These details have been previously reported. It is now reported that the victim's family has requested the defendant to provide compensation for damages, which is being handled by his family. The prosecution case has concluded, and yesterday, Judge Zhang Chaozuo presided over the First Criminal Division and sentenced Yu Guilin to four years and eight months of imprisonment for causing death through injury. The number of days in pre-trial detention will be deducted from the sentence at a rate of two days per one day of imprisonment. During the appeal period, he will be transferred to the detention center.

Another Hooligan Righteously Intervenes

A Scheduled Fight Leads to a Knife Wound

The winning side left triumphantly. His companions hired a car to send the injured man to Renji Hospital for treatment.

Kangyuan Factory Specifies Visiting Procedures

The Kangyuan Can Manufacturing Factory on Huade Road in this city has excellent equipment, meticulous management, and is known for its scientific management and has long been regarded as a model factory. General Manager Xiang Kangyuan has always embraced openness and welcomes visits from all sectors. The methods he has used are widely used as a model by various industrial factories. Since its reorganization and incorporation last year, its equipment has become more complete, and its business has flourished. There are often more than ten visits to the factory per day from people in various industries, and it is difficult to provide adequate hospitality. It is now reported that the factory has specially set visiting dates, which are from 2:00 p.m. to 4:00 p.m. every Saturday, with a maximum of ten people per group, in order to facilitate reception and avoid inconveniencing guests. Prior notice must be given to the factory, which will reply in due course. Recently, administrative agencies and university professors and students who visit have been scheduled to research solutions in batches.

Record of the Completion Ceremony of the China & South Sea Bank Building

More than 3,000 Chinese and foreign guests came to congratulate

Total daily business volume exceeded 4 million yuan

The China & South Sea Bank on Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession has been established for six years, and its business has greatly developed. The original building was therefore insufficient to meet its needs, so it invested 2 million yuan to purchase land and construct a state-of-the-art fifteen-story building. The construction took three years, with renowned Chinese and French engineers planning and building it, finally completing it. The interior is perfectly equipped, and the layout is innovative. The building was fully completed yesterday, and a grand opening ceremony was held. For a time, Chinese and foreign guests came to congratulate and deposit money, and the streets were crowded with carriages and horses. The French police specially dispatched many Chinese and foreign police and detectives to maintain order. The details are as follows:

A Glimpse of the Construction

The bank building is located in the bustling commercial district of the French Concession, reaching fifteen stories in height, and faces the road on all sides. The lower four floors on the north side are used by the bank itself, the lower two floors on the south side are shop fronts, and the nine floors above are rented out as office spaces, totaling more than one hundred rooms. Floors ten through twelve are Western-style apartments. The thirteenth floor is a staff recreation area, and the upper two floors are water towers and flagpoles. The entire building adopts the latest three-dimensional style, which is magnificent and luxurious. The bank area is particularly grand. The interior is decorated with marble. The vault is equipped with a circular vault door, and the keys are the latest style. There are six inspection rooms inside the vault for convenience. In addition to the ground floor, there is also a huge vault in the basement for rental. The office area is equipped with three elevators, and each floor has a large public reception room. The apartment area has three to five bedrooms per unit, with bathrooms, kitchens, food preparation rooms, servant rooms, and gas, electricity, water tanks, and other equipment. All projects are undertaken by famous experts, so they are highly praised by architects.

Grand Opening

The bank officially opened at 8:00 a.m. Chairman Du Yuesheng used a golden key to unlock the door, which suddenly opened, and led all the directors, supervisors, managers, and staff to enter. The bank immediately began to conduct business. For a time, people came to deposit money and open accounts. The total business volume for the day reached more than 4 million yuan.

Guests Come to Congratulate

Yesterday, more than 3,000 Chinese and foreign guests came to congratulate, including Wu Tiecheng, Yang Xiaotian, Song Ziliang, and Pan Gongzhan from the military and political circles; Chen Guangfu, Bei Songsun, Song Hanzhang, Xu Jiqing, Xu Xinliu, Tang Shoumin, Hu Bijiang, Bei Runsheng, Lin Kanghou, Sun Hengfu, and Chuan Xiaoan from the banking industry; Qin Runqing and Pei Yunqing from the money industry; and Shi Liangcai, Zhang Zhuping, Wang Boqi, Guo Le, Yu Qiaqing, Yu Zuoting, Rong Zongjing, Liu Hongsheng, Huang Jinrong, Jian Yujie, Wang Xiaolai, and others. As for foreign guests, such as French Municipal Council Director General Frasse, Directors Chapeaux and Lyder, French Police Chief of the French Concession Fabre, French Army Camp Ganber, French Deputy Consul General Lou Gan, General Manager of the Banque de l'Indochine Schleyder, and Chairman of the International Savings Society Spierling, were all warmly received by Chairman Du Yuesheng and Directors Zhang Xiaolin, Jin Tingsun, Qian Xinzhi, Li Yingsheng, Zhang Yishu, Xie Fusheng, and others, and were treated with champagne. French Municipal Council Director Chapeaux also gave a congratulatory speech, saying that the bank has not only made many contributions to the Chinese financial world, but has also greatly benefited Chinese-French trade and diplomatic relations. (Photo of the China & South Sea Bank opening ceremony taken by Datong Photo Studio)

Longhua Temple's Property Records Are All Recorded in Perpetual Account Books

The Perpetual Account Books Have Not Yet Been Handed Over

A Large-Scale Theft and Sale of Land Has Been Discovered

The former abbot of Longhua Temple, Yuan Zhao, was recently accused by Longhua Temple's mountain owner, Lu Mingzhao, and the current abbot, Xingkong, of stealing and selling temple property, requesting a thorough investigation. An order was given to detain Yuan Zhao and confiscate a small leather suitcase containing various deeds, which were transferred to the local court. Prosecutor Wu Deying questioned and detained Yuan Zhao, and summoned witnesses for questioning. These details have been previously reported. It is now understood that the court is being exceptionally cautious about this case, so it has sent a letter to the municipal party headquarters for a detailed investigation. According to records, the temple has two perpetual account books, on which all the temple's business properties, revenue-generating instruments, and solemn items are clearly recorded. One is stored at the mountain owner Lu Mingzhao's place, and the other is kept in the temple. There has been no change for a long time. Yuan Zhao took one of the perpetual account books with him when he left the temple in October of last year. He claimed to have handed it over to Zhao Yunshao, a standing committee member of the Buddhist Association, but it has not yet been handed over to the case. It has now been found that more than 30 mu of land in Xiaomuqiao area of Longhua belongs to Chengen Hall, Longhua Temple. More than 20 mu of land in Jinshan Zhujing and other places, and more than 30 mu of tidelands and reed marshes along Pujiang Beach in Longhua (the above-mentioned land is worth more than 100,000 yuan) have been almost entirely stolen and sold by Yuan Zhao. Other rare ancient bronze Buddhas and characters have also been missing in large quantities and are currently impossible to trace. Therefore, the court has been conducting thorough investigations in all directions in recent days in order to determine the facts.

The Shun'an Ship Owners Request the Customs to Move the Ship to Shanghai for Handling

In reality, it is difficult to transfer the passengers and goods first. Therefore, he has submitted a request to the Customs Administration asking if it can order the Sandu'ao Customs to release the detained Shun'an ship and order it to return to Shanghai so that this case can be transferred to Shanghai for handling.

Wu Tingsheng Returns to Shanghai to Talk About the General Situation of Xuchang Tobacco Leaves

The Color and Taste of the Tobacco are Excellent

Since its establishment, the American Tobacco Leaf Improvement Committee has been striving to improve domestic products to meet the needs of society. Its first step is to improve Xuchang tobacco leaves. The methods are divided into five steps: (1) improving tobacco varieties, (2) improving planting methods, (3) improving fertilizers, (4) improving curing methods, and (5) improving packaging. The most important of these is to improve tobacco varieties and control their production to avoid surpluses. Since this plan was formulated, Executive Committee member Wu Tingsheng has been sent to Xuchang to inspect the lives of tobacco farmers to provide research for the committee's improvement efforts. The committee also plans to purchase 100 acres of land as a test field for improving American tobacco varieties. The field will also prepare seeds and distribute them to tobacco farmers free of charge, while prohibiting tobacco farmers from storing inferior seeds. When the time for new leaves to come on the market arrived, the committee again sent Wu to inspect this year's harvest and guide tobacco farmers in adopting scientific curing methods. Wu returned to Shanghai a few days ago. According to him, this year's tobacco leaf yield was originally very rich, but a few villages suffered slight reductions in yields due to floods. However, the results in most areas are very good. In particular, after tobacco farmers adopted scientific curing methods, the color and taste of the tobacco are better than in previous years. He gained a lot of experience on this trip and is now busy drafting reports to report to the committee.

Extravagance and Keeping a Mistress Lead to a Tragic End for a Young Man

Li Runhua Commits Suicide by Poison

Li Runhua, a Yunnan native, was 39 years old and lived at No. 5 Dade Lane, at the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Carter Road. He used to work at the racecourse and had a considerable monthly income. In addition to his wife, he also kept a mistress. He was extravagant and spent money without restraint. Unexpectedly, he was soon fired, which led to a complete cutoff of income. However, Li still did not care and idled away his days as before. Soon, he was heavily in debt and unable to make up for it. Recalling the past, he was filled with resentment and committed suicide by swallowing poison in secret at dawn yesterday morning. By the time his family noticed, he was already unconscious. They rushed to report to the Xinza Police Station, which dispatched an ambulance to take him to the hospital for treatment. However, he was too deeply poisoned and could not be saved. He died in the hospital at around 10 a.m. The hospital reported the death to the police station, which transferred the body to the morgue for examination.

The Result of Gambling Addiction

Yang Zuoqi Dies Tragically from Poisoning

Yang Zuoqi, an Anhui native, was 26 years old and lived in a bungalow at No. 5 Jingzhou Road, Hudong. He worked as a mason. He was addicted to gambling and had accumulated a large amount of debt that he could not repay. As a result, he became resentful and despondent yesterday and secretly swallowed opium to kill himself. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Local Court, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, arrived at the morgue to examine the body. According to Yang Haiyun's statement, he was 45 years old and the deceased was his son. He usually gambled outside, and I repeatedly advised him, but to no avail. Yesterday morning at around 8 a.m., I saw him lying in bed crying and his face turned pale. I asked him what was wrong and learned that he had taken poison because he owed money from gambling and could not repay it. Guo obtained the statement and determined that the deceased, Yang Zuoqi, male, had died from opium poisoning. The body was handed over to his father, Yang Haiyun, who signed a statement to take it back for burial.

Huahui Offender Lin Shaoquan Escapes, the Guarantor is Discovered to Have Used a Substitute

The Substitute is Sentenced to Six Months in Prison

The Original Guarantor is Also Prosecuted

Lin Shaoquan was arrested by the French police for gambling in Huahui in the French Concession and sent to the Second Special Court for questioning. He was sentenced to one month in prison and a fine of 100 yuan. During the appeal period, he was allowed to be released on bail with a guarantor who could be summoned at any time. He then asked Zhang Shigen, a Lu'an native who ran the Hongyi Rice Shop opened by Father Lao, to sign and stamp a guarantee. However, the name of the person in charge of Hongyi Rice Shop on the guarantee was not Zhang Shigen, but Zhang Songlin. Unexpectedly, Lin absconded after being released on bail. When the case was confirmed, Zhang Songlin, the guarantor, was summoned to hand over the person within a certain period, but Zhang could not hand over the person and asked Chen Shaolang to go to court to impersonate Zhang Songlin in order to be executed in his place. However, the judge found out that Chen Shaolang was not Zhang Songlin and was impersonating him. He was immediately detained and Chen was transferred to the prosecutor's office for investigation. After the prosecution, the criminal court sentenced Chen to six months in prison. Now, the Second Special Court sent Zhang Songlin to the prosecutor's office for investigation for the crime of facilitating escape. He was allowed to be released on bail pending further instructions. Meanwhile, he was prosecuted in the criminal court. Yesterday, Judge Zhang Chaozuo opened the fifth criminal court to summon Zhang Songlin, also known as Zhang Shigen. Because Zhang had returned to Anhui for business, his lawyer, Hu Quan, appeared in court as his representative and requested a postponement. The court approved the request and ordered that the hearing be rescheduled until the defendant arrived in court.

Prostitute Accuses Customer of Abandonment After Pregnancy

Visitors to Pleasure Quarters Should be Vigilant

The Case is Dismissed

Chuan Liangzhen, a middle-aged woman of 34, used to work in a brothel. Around January of this year, she was still in a room in a brothel in Leyuli, Yunnan Road. After the Dragon Boat Festival, she moved to Shantou Road to run her own business, changing her stage name from Zhen Luolan to Hongniang, acting as both madam and prostitute. People in the brothel often called her "Guangdong Lao Er". She was very skilled at socializing and knew how to read people's minds, so those who liked to frequent brothels were happy to go to her. Kong Fanqin, the owner of the De Tai Silver Shop at No. 43 Seward Road, visited her establishment in the spring at the invitation of a friend. He was well-received, and he repeatedly came to show his appreciation. Recently, Kong stopped visiting brothels. The woman suddenly became pregnant and hired a lawyer to sue Kong in the First Special District Local Court, claiming that Kong had said that he had no wife at home and wanted to marry her, leading her to be seduced and go to a hotel with Kong for illicit sex. Now that she was four months pregnant, Kong had not fulfilled his promise and had abandoned her. She requested that Kong be punished for abandonment and attached a civil lawsuit, requesting that Kong pay 21,000 yuan for childbirth and upbringing expenses. After being accused, Kong hired lawyer Zhan Jifeng to defend himself, saying that although he had interacted with the plaintiff when she was a prostitute, there was no physical relationship. Her claim that she was a virtuous widow and that the defendant had seduced her and promised to marry her was absurd and ridiculous. Her intention was to take advantage of the fact that the defendant's reputation was at stake and that once the lawsuit was filed, his reputation would be ruined, so he would be willing to settle and pay a huge amount of money. This kind of trickery is very common in Shanghai. He requested that the court dismiss her lawsuit and punish the plaintiff for false accusation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Zehan opened the court and questioned the plaintiff, Chuan Liangzhen, about her relationship with Kong. She covered her face and cried. Kong firmly denied the accusations of seduction and abandonment, stating that the plaintiff was indeed a prostitute and that the Bureau of Public Works could be investigated. As for the money he gave her, it was for entertainment expenses and she was now making false accusations. Judge Wu had already understood the nature of the case and advised the plaintiff not to rashly file a criminal charge, saying that even if, as she claimed, she was pregnant with the defendant's child, she would have to wait until after the birth to dispute the issue of identity with the defendant. At this time, there was no abandonment to speak of. However, the plaintiff, upon hearing the advice, only stated that she was willing to withdraw the attached civil lawsuit, but wanted to proceed with the criminal lawsuit. The court immediately ordered the debate to begin. The plaintiff's lawyer spoke first, saying that since the plaintiff was pregnant, the fetus had been abandoned by the defendant, but abandoning the fetus was equivalent to abandoning the mother. Then, the defendant's lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, rebutted, saying that all the plaintiff's claims were empty and obviously intended to extort money. He requested that her lawsuit be dismissed and that she be severely punished to warn against trickery. Judge Wu immediately ruled that the plaintiff's lawsuit and counterclaim were both dismissed.

The Cotton Yarn Mill Association Will Issue a Notice to Comply with the Regulations on Banning Water Adulteration in Cotton

Statement to Cancel the Previously Established Two Articles

Formulate Measures to Ban Impurities in Cotton

The Chinese Cotton Yarn Mill Association issued a notice to its members and the cotton industry yesterday, stating that it had received a letter from the National Economic Council's Cotton Industry Control Committee stating that the Interim Regulations on Banning Water Adulteration in Cotton will be implemented from October 1. The two articles of the measures established by the association on August 29 of this year will be cancelled on September 30 of this year, and all subsequent matters will be handled in accordance with the regulations. However, regarding cotton impurities (cottonseeds, seed cotton, broken leaves, small pieces, cotton branches, sand and mud, etc.), it was decided at the executive committee meeting of the association on September 26 that those within 1.5% should be deducted in accordance with the regulations as the standard for both parties when factories purchase cotton.

New Information on Public Buses in Zhabei

A New Route 5 is Opened from North Station to the Municipal Government Dormitory

Route 3 Special Bus is Changed to Regular Bus

All to be Implemented on October 1

The original Route 4 trunk line of the Shanghai Chinese Public Bus Company ran from the North Station, via Baoshan Road, Tongji Road, Jiangwan Road, West Sports Association Road, Xiangyin Road, Songhu Road, Sanmin Road, Shiguang Road, Minfu Road, Fuhou Road, and to the left of the Municipal Government. Later, due to the obstruction of bridge construction on Sanmin Road, it temporarily ran on Guohuo Road. Now that the bridge has been completed, the Route 4 bus will be returned to the original route listed above. The company sees that construction and residents are increasing daily in Guohuo Road and other places, so in order to take into account the transportation needs of the city center, the vehicles from the North Station to the Municipal Government dormitory have been changed to Route 5. The route is roughly the same as Route 4, but from the North Station to Xiangyin Road, it relies on Guohuo Road, Fuxi Nei Road, from right to left, via the Municipal Government Building, to Fuxian Zuo Road, Fudong Nei Road, Funan Zuo Road, Haitong Road, and the Municipal Government dormitory as the temporary terminal. The fare has not changed (i.e., 53 copper coins for the entire route from the North Station to the dormitory). It is officially opened on October 1. It is also heard that the company's Route 3 special bus to Zhenru and South Gate will also be changed to a regular bus from that day. The terminal station will remain the same, but the fare and sub-stations will be handled with reference to the regular bus running on the wireless radio station. The bus frequency was originally 18 minutes from the North Station. Now that the special bus has been changed to a regular bus, it will run every 9 minutes.

Domestic Goods Manufacturers Actively Participate in the National Exhibition of the Jiangxi Provincial Capital

Since the Shanghai Chinese Domestic Goods Manufacturers Association began preparing for the National Goods Exhibition of the Jiangxi Provincial Capital, it has been actively progressing. As of yesterday, more than 90 manufacturers have participated. The details are recorded as follows:

Exhibition Registration

The association originally set yesterday as the registration deadline. In order to solicit widespread participation, the deadline has been extended by one week to October 4. As of yesterday, the participating manufacturers include Huasheng Shanghai Electric Appliance Factory, Tianchu MSG Factory, Taikang Food Company, Renfeng Textile Factory, Dingxin Textile Factory, Fuxin Cloth Factory, Limin Cloth Factory, Dachina Dachina Central Rubber Factory, Samsung Xinguang Thermos Factory, Dachina Rubber Factory, Cooperation Hardware Company, Minsheng Textile Factory, Huaou Xianghai Fine Fruit Company, Family Industry Cooperative, Yonggu Paint Factory, Yonghe Industrial Company, Shanghai Industrial Company, Dacheng Weaving Factory, Guanghua Gas Lamp Factory, Double Wheel First Brand Toothbrush Factory, Sanle Agricultural Products Cooperative, Dafeng Copper Factory, Global Minhua Umbrella Factory, Yuanchang Xin Leather Factory, Zhang Xiaoquan Gongji Yinji Xingji Scissors Factory, Yongfeng Electric Appliance Factory, and more than 90 others.

Announcement Statement

The association announced to all manufacturers yesterday that it had discovered that a printed matter resembling a notice, but not a notice, was being distributed in various places by an organization calling itself the Nanchang City Foreign Miscellaneous Goods Industry Research Association, also known as the Nanchang City Domestic Miscellaneous Goods Industry Research Institute. The wording of the printed matter seemed to oppose the association's holding of the National Goods Exhibition of the Jiangxi Provincial Capital. The reason was nothing more than that holding the exhibition of domestic goods would affect local commerce. However, because the association's holding of the Jiangxi Exhibition was initiated with the consent of the Jiangxi provincial authorities, they did not dare to openly oppose it, so they distributed this printed matter in an attempt to confuse people and sabotage it. In fact, it was a completely Monroe-style suicidal policy. The purpose of exhibiting domestic goods is to introduce domestic products and revitalize industry. Moreover, the time is short and temporary, and it will not squeeze or affect local commerce. However, the association (institute) did not examine the matter carefully and rashly issued this printed matter, which is hateful. Fearing that people would misunderstand the truth and make mistakes due to doubt, this emergency announcement is made. If there are any domestic goods manufacturers who have not participated, please come to the association to register as soon as possible. There will be no problems with the printed matter. Please do not be fooled and make mistakes. This is the announcement.

The Daxin Domestic Silk and Satin Bureau at the intersection of Shilu and Sanmarlu has decided to open on October 1. Its adopted business plan is to develop and promote the strength of domestic silk and satin. The owner of the bureau, Mr. Wang Yansong, believes that the Chinese silk industry is becoming increasingly endangered under the competition and dumping of foreign goods. This phenomenon has a very important relationship with the government's policy of saving the country through production and the livelihood of the entire nation. Therefore, in order to save the silk crisis, it is not enough to talk empty words. It is necessary to build a new camp for promoting purely domestic silk and satin to fight against the attacking foreign goods and strive to win the purchasing power of silk and satin in the Shanghai market. On the one hand, it prevents people from all walks of life who love domestic silk and satin from being deceived by foreign goods that have been disguised. On the other hand, it may arouse the attention of colleagues who also sell foreign goods to rise up one after another, abandon foreign goods, and sell only domestic silk and satin, so that the promotion force can be gradually expanded, the purchasing power can be gradually concentrated, and the invading economic foreign goods will have no skills to apply due to the loss of promotion force. This proposition is welcomed by silk and satin manufacturers in Hangzhou and Shanghai. Shi Chunshan and Lou Fengshao, representatives of Zhen Dan, Lie Feng, Zhen Ya, and other major factories, have been publicly recommended to meet with Mr. Wang Yansong to express their gratitude for his enthusiasm for planning and fighting for domestic silk and satin and to express their unanimous support. Ladies who like to use domestic silk and satin should not miss the opportunity of the bureau's opening discount.

Tenants in Dexing and Other Lanes in the French Concession Demand the Return of "Small Rent"

The Shanghai Tongren Fuyuan Hall previously built Hong Kong-style three-story buildings in Dexing Lane, Xixinqiao Street, Gongguan Road, and the original site of Qiankang Sauce Garden in 1920, and more than 200 three-story houses in Lixian and Zhizhong Lanes, Xizilaihuo Street. At that time, it had collected huge amounts of "small rent," totaling no less than 100,000 yuan, and issued receipts from the Shanghai Charity Association. As all the tenants considered the rental prices to be too high, they requested a reduction. The hall asked Wang Yiting and Lu Bohong to ask Du Yuesheng to mediate. All the rental issues were then settled. The "small rent" portion was not mentioned at the time. In recent years, the market has declined, and the tenants have been struggling to make ends meet. They have gathered with their neighbors many times to discuss the matter. Now that the Mid-Autumn Festival is over, they feel even more difficult to sustain themselves and have decided to petition Du Yuesheng, Chairman of the Chinese Taxpayers' Association in the French Concession. Yesterday afternoon at 2 p.m., four representatives from Dexing Lane, Zhai Yuchang, Qian Ziming, Cao Wenrong, etc., took a car to Du's residence on Huagene Road. After submitting their name cards, they were received by Du. Zhai Yuchang, as the representative, stated the course of events. Du replied that he was always concerned about the current difficult situation in the business community. He would convey everything to the representatives and do his best to help if he could. However, landlords and tenants have the closest relationship, and they should negotiate peacefully in the future, so that the middleman can also help easily. The representatives were very satisfied with Du's sincere attitude and thanked him before leaving. Here is a copy of their original petition to Du: Respectfully, Tongren Fuyuan Hall built more than 200 houses in Dexing, Lixian, and Zhizhong Lanes on Xixinqiao Street in the French Concession in 1920 and collected 80,000 to 90,000 yuan in "small rent." As Dexing Lane is located north of the main road and the market is more prosperous, the regulations required that 1,000 taels of silver be collected for each city house, and the rest ranged from 500 to 600 taels to 200 to 300 taels. When paying the money, Huang Xingjie, the director of the hall, publicly stated that because there were too few houses and too many people, the hall could not cope, so those who had to pay in cash were implying restrictions. Moreover, the construction cost was very high and the deposit had to be collected to offset it. After a few years, when the income was abundant, there would be a proper solution. At that time, the tenants had no contact beforehand and thought that the receipt given by the hall to the charity was sincere and reliable, but they did not know that they had fallen into its trick. Most of our tenants rent houses for profit, which is very different from donating money for charity. In short, the purpose of the hall is to collect "small rent" and it is prevented from setting up names by the ban of the Chinese and French authorities, so it tries to do so by trickery. But the contradiction is already obvious. If the market is still as prosperous as before, our tenants can still endure and remain silent. Now that the market has declined to this point, how should the great philanthropists in the name of charity stimulate their conscience to cover up their past mistakes? But the person in charge of the hall does not allow rent reductions and does not allow the return of "small rent," as if he is not happy until he sees all the tenants die under his iron fist. More than a dozen of our tenants have paid more and suffered more losses, so we have hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the Second Special District Local Court. Although the result of the lawsuit requires the final judgment of the third trial, we believe that facts speak louder than eloquence and justice is stronger than power, and our tenants will not be silent. In addition to filing a document with the Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Government Social Bureau, and various groups, we are writing to your association to uphold justice and comfort the public.

This kind of gathering is the first of its kind since the women's sports movement and will surely make a great contribution in the future.

Lake Society to Hold Memorial for Tang Jicang Tomorrow

Tang Jicang, a committee member of the Lake Society, whose given name was Zhenchang, was deeply enthusiastic about education and hygiene. He initiated the Huzhou Native Place Public School in Shanghai and established the Xun Yuan School and a Literature Specialization Department. He served as a faculty member at various schools, including Wuben Girls' School and Nanyang Middle School in Shanghai. In his early years, he participated in the revolution, braving hardships and dangers. After the Xinhai Restoration, Shanghai Governor Chen Gongyingshi invited him to serve as Secretary-General, advocating for the demolition of the Shanghai city walls and the establishment of the Shanghai Concession Merchant Corps, for which he made outstanding contributions. During the rise of the National Revolution, he devoted himself to raising military funds. After the Southeast region was pacified, he was appointed as a member of the Shanghai Special City Party Department, a member of the Shanghai Provisional Political Branch, a member of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Finance Committee and the Shanghai Finance Committee, a full-time advisor to the Shanghai Special City Government, Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Shatian Bureau, Director of the Zhejiang Saltpeter Mine Bureau, and a full-time member of the Shanghai Municipal Gazetteer Compilation Hall, Deputy Director of the State-Owned Land Management Office of the Ministry of Finance, and other positions. He regularly studied philology and promoted literacy campaigns, authoring books such as "Reading Methods," "Exploration of the Origins of Characters," "New Style National Language Textbook," "Literacy Wall Charts," "Humble Suggestions for Saving the Times," "Selections of Novels," "A Guide to Studying Statecraft," "On Mencius," "Literacy and Pronunciation," and "Examination of Chinese Character Radicals," among others. He contributed greatly to the establishment of the society. He suddenly passed away this summer. It is reported that the society is scheduled to hold a memorial service at 2:00 PM on the 30th of this month in the society's auditorium to express their sorrow.

Tianjin East Asia "Ram Brand" Wool Yarn Sells Well

In recent years, the import of foreign wool yarn into the country and the outflow of money are alarming. The Tianjin East Asia Wool Spinning Company, recognizing this, has made a thorough effort to save itself, increase production, and work towards resisting this trend. Recalling this time last year, the company's "Ram Brand" wool yarn was being promoted in Shanghai for the first time. When it was first launched, outsiders generally expected that the product, being new, would be unfamiliar to many, and that purchasing power would not be strong. They viewed it with indifference. Unexpectedly, the "Ram Brand" wool yarn caused a sensation upon entering the market, showing a sudden and rapid increase in popularity. All sectors rushed to purchase it, and it sold out completely. The reasons for this are nothing more than its careful processing, accurate weight, excellent quality and reasonable price, strong tensile strength, soft texture, and durability, among other features. It is found that the company's general manager, Mr. Song Feiqing, is experienced and has keen insights. As for Mr. Huang Gongzhan, the supervising director of the East China region, he is also intelligent and capable, and brave in taking responsibility. His supervision efforts have been quite effective. It is also reported that the company's general manager for the East China region has entrusted the Shanghai China Trade Company to handle it. The address is 17 Gongguan Road, next to Bulinli. In recent days, various distributors from different regions have been coming to negotiate wholesale purchases, with an endless stream of visitors. It is learned that last year, due to its initial creation, each skein only had twenty rounds. This year, the company has revitalized its spirit, using richer materials, and each skein has twenty-six rounds. Calculating that there are sixteen skeins per pound, this is an increase of ninety-six rounds per pound compared to last year. The special price is two yuan and eight jiao per pound, with uniform prices for both local and out-of-town sales. The purchasing power and sales volume are even greater than last year. Even in Shanghai, both the China and Shanghai National Products Companies sell several hundred pounds per day. The success elsewhere is even more imaginable.

The middle reaches of the Yangtze River and the area around here are cloudy and mostly sunny. The wind comes from the southeast to the southwest, quite strong and steep. There is fog in the morning. On the coast and East China Sea, the wind comes from the southeast to the east. The hurricane southeast of Luzon will move to the west-northwest or northwest-west. The center of the first hurricane advanced to within 120 miles of 12 degrees north latitude and 130 degrees east longitude at 6:00 AM and moved to the west-northwest or northwest-west. The center of the second hurricane advanced to within 60 miles of 17 degrees north latitude and 106 degrees east longitude at 2:00 PM and moved west. The strength of both hurricanes is unknown.
